thomas newton argument firſt epistle peter luther ¶before wee fall hande interpretation epiſtle ſhall bee verie requiſite firſt laye downe vnto reader ſome briefe admonition whereby may knowe bothe bee eſteemed alſo attaine certaine knowledge thereof firſt bee noted apoſtles doe handle one ſelf ſame doctrine therfore well done ſome ſay bee onely fower euangeliſtes fower goſpels whereas one goſpell ſo euer apoſtles haue left writyng goſpel ſignifieth nothing el preaching publiſhing grace mercie god chriſt lorde purchaſed v death take properly whiche contained bookes comprehended letter rather vocall preachyng liuely worde voyce whiche ſoundeth whole worlde ſo openly vttered maie euery bee heard neither booke containeth lawe wherein many point good doctrine hath bin hitherto commō ly beleeued draweth v confidence hope woorke owne whereby become righteous declareth vnto v riche grace god freely without owne merite giuen vnto v teachyng v alſo chriſt hauing interceſſion appeaſed ye wrath god ſatiſfied ſinnes hath quite aboliſhed blotted iniquity work iuſtified made v righteous whoſoeuer either preacheth writeth theſe thynges teacheth true goſpell deede whiche apoſtles eſpecially paule peter haue done epiſtles whatſoeuer preached publiſhed concerning chriſte one goſpell although one handle one ſorce one kinde wordes ſorce kinde thing may handled either many wordes fewe may deſcribed either briefly large howbeit ſeeyng tendeth vnto ende teache v chriſt sauiour faith hym without owne workes iuſtified ſaued al one word one goſpell one onely faith one baptiſme whole churche chriſt thou readeſt nothing written apoſtles whiche alſo contained writynges others penners scripture thei haue handled poynt eſpecially greater endeuour ſtudie reſt namely onely faithe chriſte doeth iuſtifie euen thei beſt euangeliſtes hereupon thou maieſt rightly call epiſtles paule goſpell thoſe thinges whiche matthewe marke luke haue written thei deſcribe muche beſide hiſtorie concernyng doinges miracle chriſte grace whiche chriſte hath purchaſed v none doeth fully fitly entreate therof paule eſpecially epiſtle roman ſeing word importance action doynges chriſte ſhould want one farre better deedes hiſtorie wordes doctrine followeth thoſe bookes moſt highly eſteemed whiche entreate eſpecially doctrine wordes lorde ieſus chriſte aſmuche miracle chriſt altogether ignoraūt yet wordes ſufficient v without wee ſo muche liue hereupon therefore followeth epiſtle peter bee accompted among moſte excellent bookes newe teſtament true pure goſpell aſmuche apoſtle herein teacheth nothyng el whiche paule reſt euangeliſtes doe namely ſincere faith chriſte freely giuen vnto v hauyng taken awaie ſinnes onely sauiour proceſſe epiſtle ſhall ſee ſaied wee maie likewiſe iudge bookes doctrine goſpell whatſoeuer either preached written ſorte ende maie wée boldly iudge bee goſpell haue neuer ſo faire goodly ſhewe power iudge haue al chriſtians pope councels alone whiche face crake thei none thei haue authoritie iudge doctrine thus muche maie ſuffize argument let v heare epiſtle firſt epiſtle generall sainct peter firſt chapter peter apoſtle ieſus chriſte ſtraungers dwell throughout pōtus galatia cappadocia aſia bithynia elect accordyng foreknowledge god father vnto ſanctification spirit obedience ſprinckling bloud ieſus chriſt grace peace multiplied vnto bleſſed god whiche kept power god faithe vnto ſaluation whiche prepared bee ſhewed laſt tyme wherein ye reioyce though ſeaſon neede require ye heauineſſe manifolde tentations triall faith beyng much precious gold periſheth though tried fire might founde vnto praiſe honour glorie appearyng ieſus chriſt ye haue ſeene yet loue though ye ſee hym yet beleue reioyce ioye vnſpeakeable glorious receiuyng ende faith euen ſaluation ſoules whiche ſaluation prophet haue inquired ſearched whiche propheſied grace ſhould come vnto searchyng tyme spirit whiche teſtified chriſt whiche ſhould declare ſuffrynges ſhould come vnto chriſt glorie ſhould followe vnto reueiled vnto themſelues vnto v thei ſhould miniſter thinges ſhewed vnto whiche haue preached vnto goſpell holy ghoſt ſent doune heauen whiche thinges angel deſire beholde wherefore girde vp loynes minde bee ſober truſt perfectly grace brought vnto reuelation ieſus chriſt obedient child faſhioning ſelues vnto former luſtes ignorance whiche hath called holy ſo ye holy maner conuerſation becauſe written ye holy holy ye call father whiche without reſpect perſone iudgeth according euery man woorke paſſe tyme dwellyng feare knowing ye redemed corruptible thinges ſiluer golde vaine conuerſation receiued tradition father precious bloud chriſt lambe vndefiled without ſpot whiche ordeined foundation worlde declared laſt tymes ſakes meanes doe peter apoſtle ieſus chriſt ſtraungers dwell throughout pontus galatia cappadocia aſia bithynia elect accordyng foreknowledge god father vnto ſanctification spirite obedience ſprincklyng blood ieſus beeing ſo engliſhed greeke worde 〈 nonlatin alphabet 〉 becauſe commonly knowne ſignifieth haue thought good phraze terme expreſſe tranſlate howbeeit properly ſignifieth hym declareth ſomething worde mouth mere carier letter meſſenger liuely voice deliuereth errand wordes vttereth commiſſion charge ſuche latine call oratores orator whereas thē calleth himſelf apoſtle ieſus chriſt much ſaied haue charge ieſus chriſt preache ſame ieſus chriſte vnto marke firſt thei excluded debarred whatſouer thei yt preache dreggie doatyng doctrine ſeelie fooliſhe vaine men meſſenger ieſus chriſt whiche doeth whiche chriſt hath commaunded hym preache thyng chriſtes meſſenger therefore wiſe bee heard preache whiche chriſte hath enioyned hym bee heard heare hym muche heare chriſt hymſelf beyng preſent straungers elect apoſtle wrote epiſtle thoſe country mentioned thei tyme paſte chriſtian miſerable ſubiection ſlauerie vnto turke among thou maieſt perhaps euen daie finde ſome faithfullie beleeue chriſte pontus greate large countrie bordering vpon ſea next vnto cappadocia border limites whiche twoo country almoſte conioyned hinder parte galatia former toward sea aſia bithynia ſituate toward eaſte greate large country paule preached perſonallie galatia aſia whether ye ſame alſo bithynia doe certeinly know furthermoſt two certain preache straūgers thei call forreiners namely ſuch come frō ſome place borne countrie wherein wee apoſtle calleth ſo becauſe thei gentile neither thought ſtraunge peter beeyng apoſtle iewes neuertheleſſe write alſo vnto gentile iewes call thoſe proſelites admitted ſtate iewes beeyng lineallie ſtocke blood abraham notwithſtandyng embraced iudaiſme ſubmitted theim ſelues obſeruation lawe theſe therefore apoſtle writeth gentile therefore member common wealthe iſraell beeyng conuerted faithe adioyned ſelues faithfull iewes wherefore calleth straungers elect vndoubtedly hee none otherwiſe reputeth true chriſtians theſe alone writeth whiche maner callyng theim containeth common doctrine wee ſhall hereafter large heare accordyng foreknowledge god father calleth thē elect surely ſelues accordyng ordinance god lieth owne power bryng ſelues vnto heauen haue faithe wee liſte neither god receiue heauen ſo euer naie hee verie diligently circumſpectly ſifte examine trie awaie therefore mannes doctrine free ſtrength ſelues thing dependeth god good election vnto ſanctification spirite god hath predeſtinate v holie ſpirituallie theſe woordes holie ſpirituall belligods romiſhe cleargie haue ſhameleſlie taken true profeſſors goſpell entailed ſame vnto maumetiſhe monkerie whiche ſtate thei doe call holie ſpirituall euen thei haue doen name churche ſo thei haue none pope mitred biſhops bee churche ſaiyng churche hath commaunded whereas thei meane tyme pleaſures doe determine thei liſte holineſſe conſiſteth nothyng leſſe one bee monke freere nunne bee shauelyng weare coule ſome peltyng religious habite word spirit ſignifieth ſhould holie hart inwardly ſpirite god ſaied eſpecially cauſe ſhewe nothing holie whiche god maketh holie v tyme iewes many outward ſanctifications true ſanctification thei meanyng ſainct peter god hath predeſtinate ende laſte ye ſhould bee holie deede accordyng ſainct paule ſaieth fourthe epheſians righteouſneſſe true holineſſe holineſſe whiche ſincere altogether entire ſuche outwarde holineſſe iewes nothyng eſteemed regarded god ſort doeth scripture call v holie sainctes wee beleeue beeyng yet liuyng earth rabbines papiſtes haue taken name v ſaiyng holie thei onely holie whiche heauen muſt therefore repoſſeſſe againe take notable name vnto v thou muſt needes holie yet muſt thou thinke thou haſte holineſſe thy ſelf thine owne merite thou art therefore holie thou haſte worde god kyngdome heauen thine thou art become entirely righteous holy chriſt theſe thinges muſt thou confeſſe thou wilte bee chriſtian extreme ignominie blaſphemie name chriſt ſhould ſo denie honour blood beleeue onely ſynnes cleane waſhed awaie wee ſanctified thou muſt beleeue therefore confeſſe thou art holie yet blood chriſte thine owne righteouſneſſe thou muſt doe ſuche certaintie conſtancie cauſe thou maieſt ſticke neede ſpende euen thy life boldly abide looke whatſoeuer maie herevpon come vnto thee obedience ſprincklyng blood ieſus chriſte ſorte ſaieth apoſtle commeth paſſe wee bee holie wee beleeue obey woorde chriſt ſprinckled blood ſainct peter hath vſed ſomewhat maner ſpeeche ſainct paule yet effecte muche paule ſaieth wee ſaued faithe chriſte becauſe faithe whiche maketh wee bee attentiue obediente chriſt holie worde wherefore obey word god muche bee ſubiect chriſt bee ſprinckled blood beleeue verie greeuous nature bee ſo wholie ſubiecte chriſte altogether forſlowe ceaſſe owne matter altogether neglect owne cauſes counte doe ſynnes nature therefore ſtoutly reſiſteth ſtriueth againſte doctrine yet neuertheleſſe muſt laſte ſtoupe yeeld ſelf thereunto sprincklyng read 51 pſalme sprinckle hyſop lorde ſhalbe cleane alludeth lawe moſes whence ſaincte peter tooke kinde ſpeeche thereby reuele moſes vnto v bryng v kynges highwaie rightly vnderſtandyng scripture whē moſes builded tabernacle tooke blood goates therewith ſprinckled bothe tabernacle people ſprincklyng inwardlie ſanctifie ſpirite onely outwardlie externall thinges therefore neede spirituall clenſyng foraſmuche ſanctification outward carnall whereof regarde god yet god thereby type figure ſignifie ſpirituall ſanctification whiche peter ſaieth thus muche effecte iewes pleaſe ſelues outwarde holineſſe wherby thei thought righteous good life men thei counte emong reprobate howbeit haue ſprincklyng farre better ye ſprinckled ſpirite clenſed inwardlie iewes ſprinckle ſelues blood goates outwardlie ye ſprinckled conſciences inwardly ſo harte cleane therefore herein haue greate cauſe reioyce hereof gentile bee gentile euen thoſe righteous iewes righteous ſprincklyng theſe thynges chaunged altered none ſprinklyng required whiche maie conuert v make v spirituall ſprinkle ſort nothyng el preache chriſte hath cauſe ſhed blood onely make interceſſion v vnto father ſaie moſte deare father thou ſeeſt blood whiche haue ſhedde ſynner thou doe beleeue thou art truelie ſprinkled thus thou ſeeſt true maner ſprinklyng pope monkes ſacrificyng prieſtes ſhould iumble together bryng traſhe rifferaffe baggage thei able either teache doe ſo muche peter doeth theſe fewe woordes ſubſcription epiſtle wherein declareth office whiche preacheth wherefore whiche taught onely goſpell kindes doctrine men accoumpt theim waie neceſſarie ſaluation whiche ſounde ſorte bee troden vnder feete reiected forſaken refuſed abandoned yea thoſe bookes bee loathed miſliked whiche hauyng gaie title good woorkes praiers indulgence pardon ſuche like plainlie directlie ſoundlie grounded vpon foundation grace peace multiplied vnto peter obſerueth maner whiche apoſtle paule ſalutyng vſeth although euery reſpect ſaith effect thus much ye haue peace grace perfectly therefore muſt ye continually profite vntill olde adam bee wholy killed mortified grace fauour god hath beginnyng v needefull requiſite alwaies become daily effectuall v take encreaſe euen till diyng daie acknowledgeth beleeueth fully perſwaded cōſcience god fauourable vnto aſſuredly poſſeſſed grace hart comfortably enioyeth peace ſo feareth neither world deuilles knoweth god hath power ouer al thinges fauourable mercifull vnto deliuer death hell al incommodities whatſoeuer hereupon conſcience peace within ſelf ioyfull glad doeth sainct peter wiſhe vnto faithfull true chriſtian ſalutation wherewith chriſtians ought ſalute one thus haue wee inſcription ſalutation beginneth matter epiſtle bleſſed god euen father lorde ieſus founde vnto praiſe honour glorie appearyng ieſus chriſt ye haue ſeen yet loue hym though ye ſee yet beleeue reioyce ioye vnſpeakeable glorious receiuing ende faith euen ſaluation ſoules induction preface ſee wordes nature true apoſtolicall paſtor ſuche beginnyng ſaie wherein wee maie plainly perceiue note true ſaid afore namely epiſtle amōg reſte moſte ſinguler excellencie verie entraunce hee beginneth declare chriſte benefite wee receiue hym hee ſaieth wee begotten againe god vnto liuely hope reſurrection ieſus chriſt alſo giftes beſtowed vpon v father mere mercie without deſerte theſe deede true right euangelicall phrazes theſe comfortable ſpeeches moſte meete bee publiſhed preached ala ſmall ſtoare ſuche kinde preachyng bee founde bookes euen accoūpted beſt written workes euen hierome auguſtine ſmall conſonancie agreement haue theſe wordes yet muſt ieſus chriſt bee thus preached died roſe againe hee died riſe againe men beeyng throughly moued kinde preachyng maie beleeue hym beleeuyng maie obtaine ſaluation preache true goſpell deede whatſoeuer preached ſorte goſpell whoſoeuer hee bee preacheth ſumme effect theſe woordes chriſt reſurrection hath brought v father hereby alſo sainct peter goeth euen lorde ieſus chriſte bring v father ſet hym mediator betweene god v hath bin hitherto preached wee muſt call vpon saincts bee interceſſors god hereupon wee haue runne holy virgine marie haue made mediatour leauyng chriſte meane ſeaſon angrie iudge doeth scripture commeth approcheth nerer giueth glorie chriſt lord onely mediator alone muſt come vnto father ineſtimable treaſure giuen v chriſte namely wee maie goe father aſke inheritance wherof sainct peter ſpeaketh theſe wordes doe moreouer plainly ſhewe mynde apoſtle ſo earneſtly ſuch vehement ardencie began praiſe father haue v alſo praiſe bleſſe hym incomparable rich hath giuen vnto v hath begotten v againe could euen ſo muche thinke thereof muche leſſe preuent hym ſo nothing remaining preach praiſe onely mercie god therefore boaſte workes muſt confeſſe haue onely mercie whatſoeuer wee haue lawe wrathe tyme paſt made iewes flée beyng ſtriken terror ſo durſt goe vnto mount god doeth ſtill vrge ſtrike v handleth v fauourably maie faſhionyng makyng v anewe neither giueth hee v grace doe one good woorke twoo frameth v newe creature newe life ſo wee bee thyng wee wee ſonnes adam namely wee tranſlated inheritance adam inheritance god hee maie bee father child therein heires euen good thynges hath see excellent thinges scripture handled concernyng matter inaſmuche wee regenerate ſonnes heires god wee equall dignitie honor sainct paule sainct peter holy virgin marie saincts wee haue ſame treaſure god good thynges largely otherwiſe regenerate wherefore haue chriſtians vnto liuely hope life vpō earth none cauſe ſhould help others otherwiſe beſt god ſhould euen ſtraight baptiſme receiuyng faith ende day ſuffer v dye howbeit permitteth v liue ende maie bring others alſo vnto faith ſelf hath doen v nowe wee liue earth wee liue hope albeit wee certaine faithe wee haue good thinges god faith aſſuredly bringeth regeneration ſo doeth bring alſo adoption inheritance howbeit ſee yet therefore doeth yet conſiſt hope beyng ſomewhat remoued ſight wee ſee beholde apoſtle calleth hope life hebrewe kinde ſpeeche man ſinne wee call liuely hope wherby certeinly hope aſſuredly looke eternall life whiche hid veile bee ſeene neither preſently perceiued harte faith iohn firſt epiſtle chap 3 writeth wee ſonnes god yet doeth appeare wee ſhalbe knowe ſhal appeare ſhalbe like hym ſhall ſee hym becauſe life preſent life come together neither bee wee ſhould eate drinke ſleepe watche doe workes nature life bringeth bee therewith alſo bleſſed therefore wee attaine vnto liue euer vnleſſe wee firſt dye forgoe preſent life wherefore wee liue wee muſt ſtill ſtande hope vntill pleaſe god call v hence beholde ſee thoſe good thinges hope maie come vnto liuely hope reſurrection ſaieth apoſtle ieſus chriſt dead haue oftentymes ſaied none rightly beleeue god come vnto hym without meane aſmuche wee child wrathe ſelues doe nothyng acceptable god wee haue therefore neede maie appeare hym may make interceſſion v reconcile v vnto hym none mediator lord chriſt sonne god therefore true faithe whiche turkes iewes haue ſaie beleeue god maker bothe heauen earth thus doeth deuill alſo beleeue yet doeth beleefe nothyng profite hym thei preſume come ſight god without chriſte mediator thus ſaieth sainct paule fift romanes wee haue acceſſe vnto god faithe ſelues chriſt wherefore wee muſt haue chriſte v wee muſt come hym wee muſt ſatiſfie god hym doe thinges god hym name ſame effect whiche sainct peter ſaieth place aſmuche ſaied certeinly looke eternall life although wee liue earth yet otherwiſe reſurrection chriſte ſaie euen therefore becauſe riſen againe aſcended heauen ſitteth right hande father cauſe hee aſcende might giue vnto v ſpirit whereby beyng regenerate might bee bolde goe father ſaie behold come thee mercifull father praie vnto thee putte truſt confidence praier myne owne lorde chriſt doeth make interceſſion myne aduocate theſe wordes carie ardent efficacie fierie force harte beleeueth harte beleeueth ſuche word colde neither doeth conſcience feele comfort thereby wee maie alſo iudge knowe whiche ſyncere doctrine true chriſtian preaching hee preacher goſpell muſt moſte zelouſly diligently preache forthe reſurrection chriſt whiche doeth apoſtle summe faithe thoſe bookes beſt excellenteſt whiche teache treate vpon poincte principally chiefly hath beene declared article faith moſt waightie importaunce chriſt riſen againe comforte hope vaine whatſoeuer chriſt hath either done ſuffred ſhould v ſteede therefore maner teaching moſte requiſite beholde chriſt hath dyed v taken vpon ſatiſfie v iuſtice father againſt sinne death hell moſte ſharpe bitter encountrie yet could none ouercome hym hym conquered ſubdued ſtronger roſe mawgre force brought ſubiection himſelf none cauſe ſet v free libertie daunger thraldome wee ſtedfaſtlie beleeue wee haue perfect aſſuraunce full poſſeſſion theſe benefites whiche beyng eche waie impoſſible bee brought paſſe ſelues ſtrength v behoued chriſt ſhould performe ſame otherwiſe cauſe ſhould haue deſcended heauen hither among v vile wretched ſinfull men therefore men preachyng attribute theſe thinges woorkes thei doe nothyng el cauſe theſe ſo neceſſarie pointes doctrine cannot afterwards take place harte hearer rightly vnderſtood well ought theſe thinges knowen v chriſtians throughly ought epiſtle vnderſtoode v inheritaunce immortall vndefiled fadeth awaie wee hope ſuche ſubſtaunce inheritaunce preſent wee liue hope inheritaunce whiche preſent deede immortall alſo vndefiled fadeth awaie inheritaunce wee haue perpetually without ende howbeit wee doe yet • ee ſame theſe wordes forcible wonderfull efficacie whoſe minde thei firmely fixed thinke little mooued deſire rich pleaſures worlde bee one ſhould ſo ſet minde vpon theſe tranſitorie rich delightes beleeue thoſe thynges whiche bee ſpoken worldlie wealthe terrene treaſures bee compared theſe thinges appeareth ſtraight thoſe thinges worlde endure ſmall tyme doe ſone paſſe awaie theſe thinges continue euer doe neuer faile fade moreouer thynges worlde vnpure doe defile v man ſo godly one reſpect caried away defiled vanity pleaſaunt thinges life inheritaunce vndefiled pure poſſeſſeth ſame remaineth euer immaculate finally inheritance doeth fade doeth decaie neither euer ſubiect corruption euery yearthly thyng although bée hard iron stone neuertheleſſe chaunged continueth ſtill ſoone man alſo becommeth old beautie gone becommeth lothſome vnamiable howbeit inheritance farre mutation chaunge alwaies remaineth alwaies freſhe flooriſhyng pleaſure ſo greate yearth whiche continuance become lothſome tedious ſee laſte tediouſneſſe thynges good thynges ſpoken otherwiſe whereof ſacietie euer whiche obtaine chriſt mercie god firmely beleeue thei freely giuen vnto v ſhould miſerable men owne workes merite thoſe ſo greate good thynges whiche reaſon vnderſtandyng man able ſo muche comprehende imagination harte conceiue reſerued heauen inheritaunce immortall vndefiled fadeth awaie vndoubtedly onely little remoued kepte ſight vntill theſe eye bee cloſed vpp mortall life ended ſhall certainly finde ſee ſame vnleſſe wee bee vnbeleeuyng becauſe wee ſhould doubte certaintie thereof apoſtle addeth inheritaunce whereunto corruption cleaue reſerued v heauen whiche kepte power god faithe vnto ſaluation hope ſaieth apoſtle looke excellent inheritance whereunto wee come faithe theſe doe ſorte followe one woorde wrought v faithe faithe newe birth newe birthe wee come vnto hope ſo wee certainly looke theſe thynges throughlie aſſured thereof wherefore ſainct peter fitly ſaieth theſe thynges muſt doen faithe workes apoſtle expreſſely ſaieth ye power god kepte vnto ſaluation many hauyng heard goſpell faithe onely doeth iuſtifie without woorkes doe burſt forthe ſaie wee alſo doe beleeue thinkyng bare opinion whiche thei feine vnto theim ſelues right faithe wee haue alreadie taught scripture power dooe euen leaſt good woorke without eſpeciall aſſiſtaunce god spirite ſhall wee owne ſtrength arrogate whiche moſte excellent namely beleeue theſe cogitation therefore mere dreame thinges vaine fonde god power muſt bee preſent woorke v sainct paule writeth epheſ 117 god giue vnto spirite wiſedome yee maie knowe exceadyng greatneſſe power v warde whiche beleeue accordyng woorkyng mightie power c onely god alſo certaine power doe beleue wherby wee learne leſſe matter make faithe one create againe heauen earth wee maie euidently perceiue therefore thei little knowe thei ſaie whiche vſe ſuche woordes theſe onely faithe doe ſeeyng many beleeue whiche doe good woorkes thei thinke owne imagination bee faithe faithe alſo maie bee without good woorkes wee ſaie ſaincte peter faithe power god ſoeuer god woorketh thus ſame regenerate new borne creature ſo faith naturally followe good woorkes wherefore ſhalbe needeleſſe ſaie chriſtiā doe doe good woorke foraſmuche owne accorde vnbidden worketh nothyng good woorkes howbeit bee hereof admoniſhed dooe deceiue hym ſelf falſe counterfaite ſuppoſed faithe doe therefore take regarde thoſe vaine talker prattle muche theſe thynges whoſe woordes notwithſtandyng winde • e trifle ſuch paule ſpeaketh 1 cor 4 come vnto knowe wordes puffed vp ſpirituall power kyngdome god conſiſteth woordes power power god neither true faithe good woorkes wherefore thei vndoubtedly liers whiche boaſte themſelues name faith chriſt doe notwithſtanding leade leude wicked life aſſuredly power god bee preſent thei become maner men ſuche meaneth whereas peter ſaith power god ye kepte vnto ſaluation ſurely euen faithe whiche power god beeyng v wherewith wee repleniſhed doeth woorke v thing ſo noble excellente wee haue certaine manifeſte knowledge thynges pertaine ſaluation beeyng able iudge freely pronounce thinges whiche yearth example doctrine ſincere ſounde corrupt falſe life good euill well dooen otherwiſe ſoeuer ſuche man doeth define determine ſo deede hee bee deceiued preſerued kepte power god remaineth iudge doctrine contrariwiſe faithe power god nothyng error blindneſſe reaſon caried away hither thither one woorke aſmuche ſtriueth owne woorkes come vnto heauen therefore alwaies thinketh behold bryng heauen let worke ſhall bee partaker eternall felicitie bleſſedneſſe hereupon haue ouerſpread worlde ſuche rabble ſwarmes monaſteries altar ſacrificyng prieſtes monkes frier votary ſuche greate blindneſſe doth god ſuffer fall whiche doe beleeue v beleeue hee preſerueth affordeth right vnderſtandyng thynges wee maie bee condemned blindneſſe mercie attaine ſaluation prepared ſhewed laſte tyme inheritaunce whereunto ye appoincted alreadie purchaſed beginnyng worlde prepared hid yet couered cloſed ſealed vp ſhall moment opened reueiled maie plainly ſée wherein ye reioyce though ſeaſon neede require ye heauineſſe manifolde tentations thou bee chriſtian lookeſt inheritaunce ſaluation thou muſt needes wholy depende vppon vtterly conteinne earthly thynges thou muſt alſo confeſſe openly affirme vnderſtandyng wiſedome holineſſe worlde altogether nothing wherfore thou muſt looke worlde condemne perſecute thee therefore hath sainct peter rightlie ioyned together theſe three faithe hope croſſe affliction aſmuche one theſe proceedeth howbeit giueth ſmall comfort ſuffer perſecution woordes dooe ſounde thus heauineſſe ſhall endure little afterward ye ſhall euer reioyce ſaluation alreadie prepared wherfore bee meane ſeaſon pacient affliction whiche ye ſuffer right chriſtian conſolation doctrine men doe comfort whiche haue relation bee ridde deliuered outward diſcommodities apoſtle ſpeaketh ſuche corporall comfort diſcommoditie outward trouble come good courage ſuſtaine ſuffer ye thē thinke ye maie ſhake theim bee deliuerd theim rather thinke thus ſelues mine inheritance alreadie prepared theſe affliction ſhall ſhortly ceaſe ſhall temporall comfort bée taken awaie eternall conſolation whiche wee haue god ſupplie place thereof moreouer theſe word diligently noted whiche apoſtle addeth ſaieth neede require whiche effect vttereth alſo afterward chapter 3 theſe woordes god bee ſo many men certaine force ſtriue come vnto heauen euen chruſte therefore laye vpon ſelues croſſe affliction accordyng owne opinion iudgement ſo fondlie reaſon giuen extoll owne woorkes god vtterlie diſalloweth ſuche dealyng owne woorkes whiche wee make choiſe force hym muſt looke laie vppon v ſende vnto v maie walke followe whither doeth lead guide v wherefore neede thou ſhouldeſt ſeeke procure thy ſelf affliction neede ſo require bee god thou ſhalte ſuffer chearefullie take croſſe vppon thee comforte thy ſelf hope expectation ſaluation whiche temporall eternall triall faith much precious golde periſheth though tried fire might founde c effect croſſe thoſe manifolde affictions whiche wee ſuffer life ſyncere faith maie bee knowne whiche falſe counterfait cauſe doeth lord ſo afflict v faith maie tried exercyſed made manifeſt world others alſo maie bee inuited wonne ſame faithe example wee laſt maie attaine vnto glorie wee praiſe god ſo againe alſo praiſe glorifie honour v thoſe counterfait liyng hipocrites haue contemned right waie ſhall ſubiect ſhame confuſion scripture doeth often compare croſſe vnto fire ſo sainct peter compareth gold tried fire triall faith whiche made croſſe affliction fire doeth diminiſhe golde clenſeth purifieth whatſoeuer droſſie ſubſtaunce mixed maie ſeparated ſame ſorte layeth god croſſe vpon chriſtians whereby thei maie ſcoured poliſhed well ſaied apoſtle trial faith c faith muſt tried purified euen worde pure whereunto alone ye muſt ſticke truſt vnto nothyng el purgyng ſcouryng poliſhyng v croſſe daily neceſſary v becauſe otherwiſe olde dull adam would ſtill muche hang vppon v dull ſpirite make faith vnpure suche life true chriſtian continually becōmeth better purer worde goſpell wee doe beleeue wee iuſtified beginne purged yet long fleſhe altogither cleane pure therefore doeth god caſt v middeſt fire affliction ignominie trouble whereby wee daily purged vntill ſuche tyme wee dye purgyng wee attaine vnto workes owne ſhould outwarde worke purifie harte within faith ſorte tried whatſoeuer mixed feined counterfait muſt needes bee remoued ſeparated hereupon laſt chriſte ſhall appeare ſhall followe magnificent honour praiſe glorie reioyce ioye vnſpeakeable glorious receiuyng ende faith euen ſaluation ſoules apoſtle ſaieth haue vnſpeakeable glorious gladneſſe ioye becauſe bringeth honour glorie worlde hath ſuche ioye whereof cometh ignominie ſhame sainct peter ſpeaketh true ſpirituall ioye plainly thou ſhalt reade almoſt whole scripture yet could fully vtter declare ſame theſe thing haue bin ſaied part preface wherein apoſtle ſheweth faith chriſt alſo ſame muſt proued purged aduerſities affliction whiche god doth ſende followeth faith contained promiſed scripture whiche ſaluation prophet haue inquired ſearched whiche propheſied grace ſhould come vnto searchyng tyme spirite whiche teſtified chriſte whiche ſhould declare ſuffrynges ſhould come vnto chriſt glorie ſhould followe vnto reueiled vnto wee may ſee god onely grace merit performeth thoſe thynges whiche hath promiſed hereunto tendeth whole scripture withdrawyng v al confidence work maie bryng v faith needfull diligent learnyng scripture whereby wee maie bee certein throughly confirmed faith ſame ſorte doeth sainct paule alſo call v scripture firſt chapter romanes ſaieth god promiſed goſpel afore prophet holy scripture alſo ſaieth rom 3 faith whereby wee iuſtified witneſſed lawe prophet reade alſo 17 act ſame preached faith theſſalonica whō called scripture expounded ſame vnto thē alſo ſide ſearched scripture daily whether thoſe thynges ſo ſainct paule teach behoueth v doe alſo thoſe thynges whiche reade newe teſtament wee maie learne confirme olde wherein wee ſhall ſee thoſe promiſes concernyng chriſt whereof chriſt himſelf alſo hath admoniſhed v iohn 5 searche ſaieth scripture beare witneſſe mee againe ye beleeue moſes ye would alſo beleeue wrote mee thoſe vaine ianglers therefore bee regarded whiche contemne olde teſtament preſumptuouſly ſaie wee haue neede thereof notwithſtandyng alone muſt taken foundation grounde faith ende god ſent prophet iewes thei might teſtifie vnto chriſte come wherefore apoſtles euery conuince refell iewes owne scripture prouyng ieſus chriſt cauſe bookes moſes prophet goſpels foraſmuche reade ſame thinges foretolde concernyng chriſte whiche afterwarde beyng doeu accompliſhed apoſtles preache write difference onely whereas bookes bothe committed writing yet withſtanding ſo much requiſite goſpel new teſtament ſhould contained writyng preached voyce whiche maie openly publiſhe ſounde forth maie heard euery worlde whereas alſo written neceſſary whereas olde teſtament doeth ſpeake onely chriſt come goſpel liuely word vocall preachyng chriſte alreadie come betweene bookes olde teſtament moreouer difference firſt fiue bookes moſes ſumme whole scripture peculiarly called olde teſtament hiſtories alſo bookes wherein deſcribed deedes diuers example whiche obſerued moſes lawe alſo tranſgreſſed ſame laſtly prophet whiche haue plaine relation writyngs moſes haue largely plainer wordes expreſſed ſame howbeit one ſame meaning moſes al prophetes whereas wont ſaied olde teſtament abrogated reiected thus bee vnderſtoode firſt difference betwéene olde newe teſtament wee haue ſaied olde ſignifieth chriſte come newe doeth performe exhibite preſent thoſe thynges old promiſed figure ſhadowed forth ſignified wherfore thoſe type figure doe ceaſe foraſmuche accompliſhed performed whiche thei ſignifie fulfilled thei promiſe neither ought bee obſerued hereafter choyce meates apparell place tymes thei chriſte thei referred made indifferent vſe theſe obſeruaunces ſaue iewes neither giuen ende thei ſhould thereby bee iuſtified thei ſhould ſet forth chriſt come furthermore old teſtament god double rule gouermente one inward outward gouerned people bothe inwardly harte outwardly bodie externall affaire therefore giue vnto theim ſo many lawes ſo mingled one houſehande might giue bill diuorcement wife would keepe put awaie hym pertained outward rule regiment belonged spirituall gouerment whereas god commaunded theim loue neighbour themſelues howbeit ruleth onely spiritually ouer v chriſt corporally outwardly ciuill magiſtrate wherefore chriſte come externall outward gouernment taken awaie doeth commaunde v putte difference betweene outward perſones tymes place doeth ſo gouerne v ſpiritually woorde wee lordes thynges without v bounde tyed corporall thynges thoſe thynges whiche pertaine ſpirituall adminiſtration gouernment taken awaie ſtill force thoſe thynges whiche thou readeſt moſes concernyng loue god thy neighbour theſe god haue duely obſerued lawe condemne thoſe doe beleue figure alſo haue place ſenſe spiritually thei spirituall thynges ſignified theſe outwarde figure whiche outward thynges taken awaie▪ houſebande refuſe wife adultery ſake put awaie hym whiche figure certaine ſpirituall ſignification whiche afterward ſpiritually fulfilled god ſame ſorte refuſe obſtinate iewes whiche would beleeue chriſte choſe gentile whiche dooeth euen yet alſo prouidyng refuſeth liue faithe bee caſte churche chriſt maie repente ſame ſorte conſtitution alſo wherein ordeined woman ſhould bee maried brother houſebande beyng deade bryng forthe child hym muſt bee called name hym deade poſſeſſe ſubſtaunce albeeit bee aboliſhed yet neuertheleſſe figure whiche ſignifieth ſomethyng concernyng chriſte brother hath died v aſcention heauen commaūded v ſhould goſpel make ſoules ſpouſes pregnant fruitefull hereuppon wee retaine name named hym whoſe moſte excellent rich ſucceede yet muſt boaſte ſaie haue conuerted wonne men ſuche effectes muſt onely attributed vnto chriſt ſame maie ſaied alſo figure old teſtament whiche long tedious ſeuerally rehearſe whatſoeuer olde teſtament externall outwarde yet force efficacie ſaiynges prophetes concernyng faithe loue whiche chriſt confirmeth matth 7 ſaieth whatſoeuer ye would menne ſhould doe euen ſo doe ye • hem lawe prophet moreouer moſes prophetes witneſſes chriſt beyng come tyme preache chriſt onely sauiour ſhall doe conueniently takyng place 22 chapter geneſis euill actes 15 apoſtles ſame ſorte ſhewe goſpell muſt preached gentile thei alſo might bee brought faithe bee aſſured theſe thinges therefore dooen common endeuour iewes might conuinced compelled acknowledge thynges ſo dooen thei reade foretolde scripture searchyng tyme spirite whiche teſtified chriſte whiche theim ſhould declare ſufferynges ſhould come vnto chriſt meanyng ſainct peter albeit prophecie fore ſhewed time holie ghoſt ſhould come laſt day powre spirite vppon fleſhe whiche prophecie sainct peter ſeconde chapter actes rehearſeth thereby proueth foretold tyme thoſe brother whiche liued hereby thou ſeeſt diligence alwaies apoſtles rendered reaſons thoſe thynges whiche thei preached taught approuing thē ſame scripture coū cels pope would doe thynges v without scripture cōmaundyng v obedience churche vnder paine excommunication beleue thē apoſtles repleniſhed holie ghoſte certaine bothe thei ſent chriſt alſo thei preache true vndoubted goſpell yet thei humble ſubmit ſelues thus farre thei required beleeued nothyng whiche thei proue ſoundlie scripture bee ſo thei affirmed mouthes infidel might ſtopped able ſaie nothyng againſt thē reaſon ſhall wee beleeue theſe groſſe vnlearned lubber whiche neither preache woorde god neither doe thyng iangle prate bauie reuile could yt father ſhould thus erre ſo long ſince ſo concluded wherefore theſe thinges ought reaſon giuen man wee able proue certainly scripture none ſhalbee ſaued beleeueth chriſte ſo theſe men able ſpeake thyng againſte alſo thei ſhall neuer bee able proue vnto v childiſhe trifle scripture namely damnable eaſe whiche faſteth daie ſuche like wherefore meete neither ought wee hande beleeue sainete peter ſaieth moreouer glorie ſhould followe whiche ſpoken apoſtle maie bee vnderſtoode bothe affliction whiche chriſt ſelf ſuffered alſo thoſe wee chriſtians member doe ſuffer ſainct paule calleth ſufferyng chriſte whiche euery chriſtian doeth ſuffer affiance name worde woorkes chriſte myne foraſmuche firmely beleeue ſo affliction alſo aſmuche afflicted ſake wherefore affliction chriſt daily accompliſhed chriſtians euen vnto ende worlde ſmall comfort vnto v howſoeuer thinges fall wee certaine affliction ſo common togither chriſte v counteth otherwiſe owne alſo maie little encreaſe comforte glorie ſhall vndoubtedly followe theſe affliction howbeit wee muſt knowe alſo chriſt came vnto glorie hee ſuffered ſo wee alſo muſt firſt beare croſſe hym maie afterwardes reioyce togither thinges therefore ſaieth apoſtle effect whiche wee dode preache prophetes haue long ſince manifeſtly declared foretolde thei ſhould come paſſe holie ghoſte reuellyng ſame vnto whereas wee doe ſo little vnderſtande prophetes cauſe wee ignorant tongue wherin thei write thei haue written plainly manifeſtly wherefore ſkilfull tongue haue spirite god whiche vndoubtedly beleeue haue harde vnderſtande muche thei know unto whole scripture tendeth bothe tongue vnderſtood ſpirite wantyng appeareth otherwiſe prophetes madde dronken howbeit wee ſhould want either theſe farre better haue spirite without tongue tongue without spirit prophetes ſpake ſorte apoſtles yet ſignifie ſame thinges afterward vnderſtandyng hereof wee might learne ſame maiſters thus haue wee ſure helpe ſtrengthenyng faithe better inſtruction whereby wee maie bee able defende ſelues againſt falſe doctrine whiche thinges angel deſire beholde greate thinges haue apoſtles delared vnto v holy ghoſte whiche came downe vppon heauen euen angel doe deſire beholde ſee wee muſte greate attention ſhut eye ſee goſpell wherein ſurely haue exceedyng delight ioye conſolation yet ſee theſe thynges bodily eye wee muſt beleeue wee made partaker righteouſneſſe truth ſaluation good thinges god hath inaſmuche hath giuen vnto v chriſte onely begotten sonne fountaine head good thinges ſhould hee hym giue v alſo good thynges rich treaſures whereat angel heauen doe take merueilous ioye delight theſe thynges offered vnto v goſpell ſo beleeue muſt needes likewiſe take merueilous delight pleaſure therein howbeit delight pleaſure wee liue earth cā ſo perfect angel beginneth v ſo faith wee haue certein feelyng thereof heauen ſhall bee ſo greate harte man able comprehende yet ſhall enioye ſame come thither thus thou ſeeſt saincte peter teacheth v arme prepare ſelues scripture hitherto hath deſcribed preache goſpell foretolde prophetes ſhould bee ſorte preached taught hee proceedeth hereafter exhorteth v faithe embrace loue followe ſuche preachyng goſpell ſaiyng wherfore girde vp loynes mind bee ſober truſt perfectly grace brought vnto reuelatiō ieſus chriſt obedient child faſhioning ſelues vnto former luſtes ignorance whiche hath called holy ſo ye holy maner conuerſation becauſe written bee ye holy holy exhortation faith meaning wherof foraſmuche ſo greate thynges preached giuen vnto goſpell whiche euen angel doe deſire pleaſure beholde ſee ye faithfully cleaue vnto aſſured truſt affiance repoſe hope therein faithe maie bee ſincere ſounde fained opinion dreame girde vp loynes mynde sainct peter ſpeaketh ſpirituall girdyng mynde like man ſhould corporally girde ſworde vppon loynes girdyng chriſt maketh mention luke 12 ſaieth let loynes girded ſome place scripture loynes ſignifie carnall luſt concupiſcence ſainct peter ſpeaketh spirituall loynes whereas scripture ſpeaketh bodie calleth part loynes whence father proceedeth naturall generation according read gen 46 chriſt ſhould ſpring loynes iuda wherefore corporally girde loynes ſignifieth nothing el chaſtitie eſay chap 11 righteouſneſſe ſhall girdle loynes faithfulneſſe girdle reynes onely faithe filthie vnlawfull luſt reſtrained brideled ſpirituall girdyng whereof apoſtle ſpeaketh ſorte virgin bodie chaſt entire ſo mynde faithe whereby eſpouſed chriſt ſpiritually ſounde ſincere howbeit ſone reuolteth faithe falſe erroneous doctrine violate corrupted wherevppon scripture commonly calleth infidelitie idolatrie name adulterie fornication namely mynde ſticketh doctrine mē forſaketh faithe chriſt sainct peter dehorteth hee biddeth girde vp loynes mynde effect aſmuche ſhould ſaie ye haue heard goſpell attained vnto faithe ſee ye perſiſt therein ſuffer ſelues defiled corrupted falſe doctrine waueryng vncertentie waie waie apoſtle ſainct peter vſeth certen peculiar proper kinde ſpeeche ſuche ſainct paule vſeth ſaith gird vp loynes mynde hee calleth mynde otherwiſe call thought ſaie thinke thus right ſainct paule ſaieth ſo dooe wee thinke ſuche opinion ſo ſeemes vnto v meanes doeth apoſtle moſte properly ſignifie faith meanyng thus much effect ye haue attained true thought ſetled right perſwaſion wee iuſtified faithe onely perſiſt ſtrongly herein girde faſt vnto valiauntly ſticke thereunto let man pull theſe ſounde opinion harte ſhall yee proſperouſly perſener ſtande many falſe teacher ariſe forge doctrine men thereby corrupte mynde looze girdle faithe wherefore harte receiue admonition whiche giue aforehande doctrine truthe maie well fixed mynde maie valiauntly perſiſte therein thoſe hypocrite whiche truſte woorkes liue honeſt vertuous life appeareth outwardly dooe verily thinke fully perſwaded god muſte needes receiue theim heauen becauſe woorkes maketh proude preſumptuous glorious owne conceiptes phariſey mentioned 18 luke whereof alſo marie maketh mention ſong commonly called magnificat ſhe vſeth ſame woorde whiche thou readeſt sainct peter hath ſcattered proude imagination harte hath ouerthrowne brought confuſion deuiſes owne myndes thoughtes bee ſober sobrietie perteineth outwardly bodie eſpeciall woorke faithe although manne bee iuſtified yet free euill deſires deede faithe hath begonne reſtraine bridle fleſhe notwithſtandyng ſame doeth continually ſtriue againſt aſſaulteth ſondrie ſortes deſires whiche goe aboute accordyng concupiſcence thereof againe burſt forthe preuaile wherefore spirite hath daiely muche adoe bridle reſtraine muſt therefore without intermiſſion haue continuall fight alwaies take greate heede fleſhe leaſt tyme ſuche craftineſſe thereof vndermine ſupplant faithe premiſſes appeareth farre thei deceiue theim ſelues whiche boſte thei haue faithe coumpt ſufficient liuyng meane ſeaſon according owne luſtes deſires true faithe muſte needes bee earneſt endeuour keepe bodie vnder holde bridle outragyng doyng liſteth herevpon ſainct peter exhorteth v bee ſober howbeit biddeth v deſtroye bodie weaken meete ſome haue doen whiche haue made ſelues mad ouer muche faſtyng yea ſome haue quite pined conſumed themſelues waie fonde error tyme ſainct bernard although otherwiſe holy man afflicted bodie ſo great abſtinence reaſon noyſome breathe whiche hee gott thereby man could abide ſtande neere hym bee companie hee length deliuered error willed brother thei ſhould much pine pinche body well ſawe vndue abſtinence made himſelf vnfit ſerue brother wherefore sainct peter requireth wee ſober wee doe ſo muche ſo farre reſtraine fleſhe wee feele wantonneſſe vnrulineſſe thereof require hee appointeth certen tyme pope hath doen long wee muſt faſte leaueth euery one iudgement ſo faſt hee bee alwaies ſober hee doe ſo ſurcharge bodie ouermuche eatyng drinking maie haue perfect vſe reaſon knowe vſe ſenſes aright liue profitably beneficially others vocation prepoſterous abſurde vnprofitable thyng giue generall precept hereof vnto whole people churche aſmuche wee vnlike among ſelues one hath ſtrong bodie another weake ſo needefull one abſteine muche abſteine little bodie maie neuertheleſſe remaine health bee fit doe good workes againe bee ſome deale cleane contrarily thinke thei doe well faſtyng nothyng ſuppoſyng thei maie without reſpecte tyme eate thei herein thei doe well albeit thei haue ſomewhat taſted goſpell yet haue thei profited little nothyng like vnto former thei haue profited onely contemne lawes pope thei girde vp mynde ſenſes peter biddeth neither thei bridle deſires bodie ſluggiſhneſſe laſciuiouſneſſe thereof maie bee repreſſed good faſte howbeit right faſte deede giue bodie nouriſhmente needefull preſerue healthe alſo exerciſe labour watchynges leaſt old aſſe become wanton laſciuious meete let hym bee reſtrained bridled obedient spirite whiche saincte peter calleth bee ſober ſome wont faſte ſo exceſſiuely engorge pamper ſelues fiſhe beſte ſortes wine one diner thei make beallies like taber drumme ſtuffyng crammyng ſo full truſte perfectly grace brought vnto svche chriſtian faithe affiaunce wholie truſteth woorde god quietly committeth ſelf vnto confidently attempteth whatſoeuer teacheth whereupon peter ſaith loynes mynde girded vp faith ſincere ſounde ye doe quietly confidently commit ſelues worde god bolde vpon truſt therein hauyng regarde whatſoeuer thyng commeth perill whether bee rich good name bodie euen life ſelf excellently therefore hath theſe wordes deſcribed ſincere vnfeined faithe faithe muſt ſluggiſhe ſleepie whiche rather dreame faithe muſt bee liuely effectuall ſo one would confidence offer ſelf affliction trouble whatſoeuer depende wholy woorde eſteemyng indifferently whatſoeuer ſtate god ſendeth wee maie patiently ſuſteine aduerſitie well enioye proſperitie example ſake muſt dye muſt confidently commit ſelf chriſte muſte quietly offer life ſake truſtyng woorde whiche deceiue muſte boldly couragiouſly triumpht ouer myne aduerſaries needfull moreouer faith ſhould paſſe without declinyng waie ſuffer ſelf hindered terrified meanes remoue frō eye whatſoeuer ſeeth heareth feeleth suche faithe doeth sainct peter require whiche conſiſteth thinkyng woordes mightie power effectuall vertue ſaieth ſainct peter truſt perfectlie grace brought vnto ſaie haue deſerued exceadyng greate grace euen freelie offered brought vnto goſpell whiche declareth publiſheth grace vnto v wée ſelues haue neither deuiſed found holie ghoſt hath ſent frō heauen worlde thyng brought vnto v forſooth euen thinges whiche wee haue afore mentioned namelie whoſoeuer beleeueth chriſte cleaueth faſte vnto woorde hath together hym benefites bleſſynges whiche bee his▪ ſo muche thereby euen lorde ouer synne death deuill helle moſte certainly aſſured euerlaſtyng life ſo greate treaſure brought home v owne doores laied vp boſomes without owne helpe merite deſeruyng yea euen vnhoped vnlooked neither knewe ſo muche thought ſuche matter▪ therefore apoſtle exhorteth v wee ſhould boldlie vndoubtedlie looke grace becauſe god whiche offereth beſtoweth ſame vpon v wiſe lye reuelation ieſu chriſte god offereth grace none chriſt therefore without mediatour lette mā preſume come ſight haue afore admoniſhed heare manne hym bryngeth hym chriſte moſte deare sonne bee aduocate spokeſman one onely hath reſpecte vnto ſake thoſe faithe cleaue faſte vnto hym therefore requireth handes acknowledge sonne perſone whoſe blood wée one hym dare preſent ſelues hym ende came lord chriſt taking fleſh blood vnto ioyned hymſelf v hee might obtaine pardon purchaſe grace v yt hādes father faith chriſt prophetes patriarch ſaued behooued menne generally beleeue promiſe made vnto abraham thy ſeede ſhall nation bee bleſſed therefore iewes turkes thei repoſe truſte owne workes hopyng thereby winne heauen haue faithe therefore dooeth peter ſaie grace brought yet reuelation ieſu chriſte ſpeake plainly ieſus chriſte reuealed vnto goſpell ſhewed vnto v chriſte maie throughly knowe hym namely sauiour taketh awaie sinnes deliuereth v miſeries reconcileth v vnto father without workes doeth iuſtifie ſaue v ſoeuer doeth thus acknowledge chriſt altogether deceiued albeit thou knowe hym bee sonne god died roſe againe ſitteth right hande father yet haſt thou thereby throughly knowne chriſt neither ſhall knowyng hym whitt auaile thee vnleſſe thou proceede ſteppe bothe knowe alſo beleeue theſe thynges thee helpe relieue comfort thee vaine therefore al thoſe thynges whiche hitherto haue obtruded preached vnto v schoolemen inſomuche thei without knowledge chriſt entred commonly conſideration thereof onely thinke muche ſorrowe greef lorde chriſt ſuſtained paſſion though ſitteth idle heauen takyng care v ioiyng hym ſelf whereby people harte remaine vtterly drie without right vſe heauenly dew water ſoules ſo liuely faithe growe take roote chriſte ought thus bee preached liueth raigneth hym ſelf wiſe neede hym deſcende worlde ſhedde precious blood sith ſent worlde hym worlde might bee ſaued hymſelf third ihon declareth needefull ſhould accompliſhe performe ſelfſame thyng whiche ſent father woorde ſent commyng vnderſtoode diuine nature chriſte onely rather humaine nature office whiche bore executed immediately baptized beganne deale office doe wherevnto ſent whiche came worlde namely ſhewe declare truthe vnto menne many beleeued hym ſhould bee ſaued ſorte therefore hee openly publiſhed hymſelf woorkyng meanes might knowne offring grace owne ſelf vnto v obedient child behaue ſelues becommeth obedient child obedience scripture ſignifieth faithe pope doctorlie schoolemen cloiſtered diuines hath gloſes mangled woorde wreſted maintenaunce lye trifle thei haue dooen whatſoeuer el reade scripture concernyng obedience namely notable ſaiyng 1 reg 15 obedience better sacrifice thei ſawe highlie obedience commended scripture thei haled forced ſame proper vnto theim ſelues thereby blinde worlde bryng menne errour thinke obedience ſo greatly commended scripture nothyng el embrace allowe ſoeuer thei ſhould enioyne laie vppon theim meanes doe thei drawe v woorde god liyng legendaries deueliſhe obedience whereas deede obedient child god heareth goſpell woorde god faithe embraceth ſame therefore whatſoeuer woorde giue eare vnto rather ſtampe tread vnder thy feete faſhionyng ſelues vnto former luſtes ignoraunce bee thoſe maners neither haue ſuche conuerſation aforetyme haue let man ſee life whiche heretofore haue ledde liued heretofore idolater liued luſte surphette drunkenneſſe couetouſneſſe pride wrathe enuie hatred whiche euill heathenniſhe life yea rather mere infidelitie deſperate forlorne conuerſation walked blinde ignoraunt wottyng therefore put ye awaie theſe euil deſires thou ſeeſt imputeth theſe miſcheeues vnto ignoraunce vnto spring thei procede flowe perfect faithe true knowledge chriſt lackyng nothing el errour blindneſſe ſo menne liue vtterly ignoraunt right wrong thereby runne headlong without ſtoppe ſtaie miſcheeues inconueniences ſort hitherto haue wee dealt withall chriſte darkened almoſte aboliſhed baniſhed worlde ſteede truthe wee nozzeled errour place ſincere knowledge truth wee faſt chained clogged ignorance ſo muche within queſtion mooued debated worlde ouer meanes wee might attaine felicitie infallible ſigne blindneſſe ignoraunce ſincere knowledge faithe extinct taken awaie herevpon grewe worlde peſtered ſuche number sectes thynges torne ſonder diſordered euery manne framed owne imagination peculier ſeuerall waie hymſelf heauen euill ſith wee able waie helpe ſelues wee chooſe alwaies bee drowned deeper deeper gapyng gulphe vtter blindeneſſe therefore ſainct peter woordes ſhould ſaie haue long inough walked fooliſhneſſe caſte ſame awaie beeyng wiſe hauyng raught vnto true knowledge whiche hath called holie euen ſo bee ye holie maner conuerſation becauſe witten bee ye holie holie doeth sainct peter hymſelf dutifully eche reſpect behaue ſelues towardes hym frame theim ſelues ſeruiceable herevpon falleth lorde god holie ſo alſo ſhould people bee holie walke faithe verie little mention made scripture sainctes holie men departed life alwaies maner ſpeaketh thoſe holie menne yet aliue prophet dauid pronounceth himſelf holie 86 pſalme ſaiyng preſerue thou soule lorde holie ſmatteryng doctorlie diuines schoolemen haue alſo miſconſtrued peruerted true ſenſe place ſaiyng prophete hath peculier reuelation calleth himſelf holie wherein thei flatly bewraie themſelues bothe lacke faithe alſo vtterly vnacquainted reuelation chriſt thei thei might eaſely effect feele ſelues power therof chriſtian hath feelyng ſuche reuelation conſcience hath feelyng ſame chriſtiā chriſtian commeth communion chriſt partaker goodneſſe therfore ſeyng chriſt holie member muſt alſo needes holie el deny chriſte holie thou bee baptized thou haſte put garment holineſſe whiche chriſte ſainct paule teſtifieth worde holie ſignifieth whiche onely proper vnto god himſelf hym onely doeth appertaine commonly doe call conſecrated therefore doth ſainct peter ſaie haue conſecrated ſelues vnto god therefore ſtandeth vppon ſo looke ye ſuffer ſelues bee caried awaie againe vaine luſtes deſires worlde giue place vnto god hee maie raigne liue woorke ſo ſhall ye bee holie euen hee holie thus hath hitherto deſcribed grace offered vnto v goſpell preachyng chriſte hath taught v againe ought behaue ſelues toward ſame namely perſiſt continue pure ſincere perſwaſion faithe well aſſured worke whatſoeuer either doe deuiſe thing auaile v toward ſaluatiō doctrine preached ſtraightwaies reaſon commeth inferreth thus caſe ſo ſtande neede haue doe good worke doe theſe groſſeheads enter fonde opinion rather mere madneſſe makyng right chriſtian life carnall licentiouſneſſe deemyng lawfull euery man dooe liſteth ſuche maner perſones doeth ſainct peter place meete withall preuention taketh aforehande fooliſhe imagination teachyng v chriſtian libertie without dependyng vpon good workes bee vſed towardes god becauſe hym onely build faithe without workes hereby wee attribute vnto hym due due honour acknowledge hym good god bothe iuſt true mercifull suche faithe deliuereth offereth v frō ſinnes miſchéeues whatſoeuer haue attributed vnto god al reſidue liues haue liue beſtowe benefite neighbor ſerue doe good vnto hym cheefeſt principalleſt worke others proceeding iſſuyng faith mouthes readie confeſſe chriſt bloud alſo beare witneſſe vnto hym caſe ſo require beſtowe liues alſo ſake yet hath god neede ſuch worke therefore muſt wee doe faithe beyng thereby throughly tried manifeſted maie alſo drawe allure others like furthermore bee woorkes dooe generallie alſo ſerue ende wee maye thereby doe good vnto neighbor whiche notwithſtandyng wee ſelues god hee muſt worke bryng ſame paſſe v thus haue wee nothyng worlde owne wee aſcribe reſpecte vnto ſelues hereby euidently appeareth farre preaching goſpell doeth open yea neuer ſo little windowe liue carnallie euery man maie lawfullie doe liſteth therefore ſaieth sainct peter furthermore ye call father whiche without reſpect perſone iudgeth according euery man woorke paſſe tyme dwellyng feare knowyng yee redeemed corruptible thinges ſiluer golde vaine conuerſation receiued tradition father precious bloud chriſt lambe vndefiled without ſpot whiche ordeined foundation worlde declared laſte tymes ſakes whiche meanes dooe beleeue god raiſed dead gaue glorie faithe hope might god meanyng ſainct peter place ye faithe come poinct ye sonnes god father ye haue attained incorruptible inheritaunce whereof hath beene ſpoken afore therefore remaineth nothing behind veile taken awaie may bee openly ſhewed earſt hidden muſt ye yet expect looke till tyme come bee giuen ſee therefore come good poinct maie boldneſſe truſt inuocate call vppon god father becauſe neuertheleſſe iuſt render vnto euery one without reſpect perſones accordyng workes let man perſwade hym ſelf dignified entitled worthie name bee called chriſtian sonne god therefore god ſpare hym hee liue without feare accoumpt enough becauſe hee hath ſuche excellent name worlde deede iudgeth accordyng reſpectes perſones iudgyng perſones equallie indifferently ſpareth ſuche bee freendes wealthie riche fayre learned wiſe mightie high authoritie god reſpecteth none theſe hee dealeth thynges indefferencie bee perſones neuer ſo high callyng hee egipt ſlea childe aſwell kyng pooreſt sheepeheard exod 10 therefore apoſtle warneth v wee lookyng like seede abraham people god scripture maketh difference accordyng fleſhe according spirit true god promiſed chriſt ſhould borne ſeede abraham hym ſhould come holie people followeth therevpon bee child god whiche deſcended ligne abraham hee alſo promiſed ſaluation gentile ſaied hee would ſaue gentile ariſeth queſtion ſay god doeth ſaue v onely faithe without reſpect good workes happeneth sainct peter doeth ſaie hee iudge accordyng perſon according euery man worke anſwere whatſoeuer wee haue taught concernyng faithe alone doeth iuſtifie v god without al doubt true foraſmuch scripture declareth witneſſeth ſame plainly bee denyed whereas ſainct peter doeth ſaie god iudgeth accordyng workes alſo true waie muſte vndoubtedly bee beleeued faithe neither good woorke bee againe faithe bee good workes therefore thou muſte bryng bothe thy faithe thy good woorkes one bothe together comprehended contained ſumme true chriſtian life thou liueſt therefore ſo ſhalt thou receiue ſo god iudge thee therfore although god iudge v accordyng woorkes yet neuertheleſſe remaineth alſo alike true good workes onely fruictes faithe whereby ſhalbe eaſie finde trie faithe infidelitie therefore god iudge thée accordyng thy workes thereby laie face face thy charge whether thou haue faithe man better confute lyer owne woordes yet neuertheleſſe plaine thoſe word made lior lyer afore vttered lye becauſe lye muſt needes proceede harte mouth take therefore theſe ſame woordes sainct peter moſte ſimple ſenſe ſuch ſorte vnderſtande workes fruictes ſeales faithe god doth iudge men according theſe fruictes whiche enſue followe true ſounde faithe intent maye manifeſtly appeare faithe remaineth harte alſo infidelitie lodgeth god iudge accordyng theſe interrogatory queſtions whether thou called chriſtian whether thou bee baptized hee thus queſtion thee sirrha thou bee chriſtian bee thy fruictes whereby thou art able confirme approue thy faithe therefore ſaieth ſainct peter foraſmuche haue whiche thei vſed externall outwarde applied outwardlie inwardly deede diſeaſe harboured thei could ſerue ſufficient able maiſter kill thoſe deſires mynde whiche thei warred peter place ſheweth v moſte spirite ſaie neceſſarily behooueth onely reade heare worde god embrace ſame harte therefore enough goſpell bee preached heard thou muſt continuallie cleaue vnto followe grace hath worde oftner man brotherly without fainyng ende muſt wee leade chaſt life ende thereby attaine saluation forſooth ende purpoſe wee maie ſerue doe good neighbor ſhall doe maie reſtraine keepe vnder sinnes muſt profite doe good others loue one pure harte feruently holie apoſtles peter paule doe ſeparate make difference betwene brotherly loue commō loue brotherhood yt bond wherein chriſtians ought among themſelues euen brother without reſpect difference haue common one chriſte one baptiſme one faithe one treaſure bee worthie thou whiche thou haſte alſo haue finallie euen riche thou wee haue one ſame treaſure ſauyng peraduenture receiue worthily thou doeſt ſhould laie vpp gold thou ſhouldeſt kepe ſome filthy rag viſe cloute therefore wee haue grace chriſte ſpirituall bleſſynges common together ſo alſo ought haue body liues wealth dignity common one one maie ſerue others turne neceſſitie thinges hee verie ſignificantlie ſaieth loue brotherly without fainyng without gloſing hypocriſie diſſimulation whiche terme phraze apoſtles gladlie vſe vndoubtedlie thei foreſawe wee would ſticke call one chriſtian brother yet would falſly feinedly diſſemblyngly altogether hypocritically vndermine one haue erected world many fraternity brotherhoodes whiche deede nothing el ſtarke vanity mere deceiptes altogether deuiſed inuented brought world deuill himſelf whiche wholy altogether paltrie counterfaited hypocriſie thou ſpeakeſt chriſte abide ſuche trumperie brooke none common brotherhood whiche haue altogether wilt thou plaie notorious foole breakyng erecte make thy ſelf newe brought forthe power owne worlde muſt firſt begotten borne carpenter able owne arte make tree ſame muſt needes ſelf firſt grow groūd therfore euer made borne sonnes child adam haue naturally ſucked office neuertheleſſe haue one ſhould haue power abſolutely reſt therefore ought man intrude hymſelf take vpon preach congregation behooueth bee choſen churche bee thereto appoints 〈◊〉 admitted againe higheſt prieſte god wee alſo muſt needes prieſtes alſo whatſoeuer hath haue theſame wherefore would wiſhe worde prieſt well name chriſtian ſhould bee common theſe name prieſte chriſtian baptized one abide theſe popiſhe shauelynges ſhould thus preſume take vpon onely good chriſtians onely baptized neither ought ſuffer thei would onely haue ſelues bee prieſtes although notwithſtandyng thei haue violently haled pulled worde pertinently properlie ſpoken vnto theim euen like preſumption brainleſſe boldneſſe thei haue called onely churche whiche pope mured crewe hath hitherto concluded decreed scripture teacheth v maner leſſon therefore diligentlie note marke theſe thynges ende thou maieſt throughly diſcerne betweene theim whom▪ god calleth prieſtes theim ſo call theim ſelues meanes long miſtakyng wee muſt length recouer reduce woorde prieſte right ſenſe proper meanyng maie bee common name name chriſtian bee prieſt name outward externall office ſuche exerciſed onely towarde god spirite euen ſelf ſame maner wee indifferently called kinges euen prieſts ſo alſo kinges place spirituall vocable woordes like alſo theſe name chriſtian holie churche euen thou doeſt cal man chriſtian becauſe hath muche money wealthe becauſe beeyng builte vpon aforeſaied stone beleeueth chriſte likewiſe art thou therefore called prieſte becauſe thou haſte ſhauen croune ietteſt ſtreates long goune becauſe thou dareſt appeare ſhewe thy ſelf ſight god offryng vp thy ſelf vnto hym praiyng whole churche vnto thou bothe canſt vſeſt preache chriſte verie ſame maner altogether thou arte therefore kyng becauſe thou weareſt croune golde haſt large dominion many people vnder thee ſubiection becauſe thou art lorde thinges yea ouer death sinne hell thou art aſwell kyng chriſt hymſelf kyng ſo bee thou beleeue hym kyng ſuche ſorte kynges worlde neither weareth croune golde neither rideth pompouſlie abroade glitteryng traine gallaunt horſes yet neuertheleſſe kyng kynges hath kynges vnder power iuriſdiction ſpeake thynges muſt ſubiect vnder feete behold euen ſo greate ſuche lorde art thou thou beleeue hym ſoeuer hath ſame alſo thyne might ſome peraduenture obiecte thus vnto ſaie saincte
