true loue deede wee knowe thei ſlaunder raile backbite v accoumpt v better leude naughtie perſons therefore ſtandeth v vpon behaue ſelues ſo orderly honeſtlie decentlie conuerſation thei beyng enforced ouercome truth maie reporte ſaie surely theſe fellowes worthily charged notorious wickedneſſe read emperours perſecuted chriſtians thei could burden odious crime laie thing charge onely thei worſhipped chriſt honoured hym god maie appeare certain letter thereof written plinie vnto traiane emperor wherein hee ſpecifieth hee could perceiue harme ill behauiour chriſtians ſauyng onely euery mornyng daylight thei aſſembled together ſong pſalmes vnto god chriſte thei eate together wit holie communion euchariſte miſdemeanours cōfeſſeth cleare vnaccuſable therfore ſaieth ſainct peter place muſt paciently beare though thei raile backbite euill doer therefore ſo much rather ought narowlie looke conuerſation ſo vnblameablie liue ye giue cauſe offence none meanes ſhall length bring thus ſeeyng honeſt behauiour abandon former naughtie life frame themſelues better daie viſitation ought ſo long ſuffer thē ſlaunder ſpeake euill vntill truth thinges burſt come light thei ſhall openly beholde ſinceritie dealinges ſhall plainly ſee haue ſlaundered ſhall therby beginne glorifie god submitt ſelues vnto maner ordinaunce man lordes ſake whether bee vnto king vnto ſuperiour vnto gouernours vnto ſent puniſhment euill doer praiſe doe well ſo god well doyng ye maie put ſilence ignorance fooliſhe men free hauyng libertie cloake maliciouſneſſe ſeruantes god honor al men loue brotherly fellowſhippe feare god honour kyng ſort proceedeth ſainct peter orderly methode teachyng v maner perſones wee ought ſhewe ſelues eche reſpect hitherto hath reaſoned generalitie euery ſeuerall condition life wee ſhould frame ſelues direct conuerſations inſtructeth teacheth v wee ſhould behaue ſelues towarde ciuile magiſtrate ſeyng hath alreadie afore declared firſt dooe god secondly wee deale ſelues ſaie fleſhe laſtly alſo teacheth v doe performe men generall therefore meanyng firſt haue performed theſe vniuerſall generall dueties whiche haue afore layed downe vnto wit walkyng true faithe towarde god bridelyng chaſtiſing bodie waxyng wanton laſciuious next chiefeſt poinct whiche require vnfeinedly hartily performe obedient vnto magiſtrate vnto lawes ſet doune law statute god enacted v humbleneſſe reuerence faith obeied ſo alſo certaine humaine worldlie ordinaunces decree conſiſtyng lawes proclamation quiet politique gouernance common wealthe vnto whiche statute wee alſo ought bee obedient submitt ſelues vnto maner ordinaunce man lordes ſake whether bee vnto kyng vnto superiour vnto gouernours vnto ſent hym puniſhment euill doer praiſe doe well obedience whiche wee duetie owe vnto ciuile magiſtrate ſaieth ſainct peter owne ſakes god ſake whoſe childrē bee whiche obedience vnto magiſtrates dutifully exhibite without hope merite rewarde whatſoeuer doe god ſake ought doe freely ſake inſomuche ſhould nothyng whiche knowe bee agreeable conſonant wil yt deſirous moſt willing allowe doe ſame ought abene magiſtrate god ſake forſooth becauſe good wil god puniſh wicked euill doer defende protect maintaine good vertuous therby concorde may bee eſtabliſhed worlde whiche publicke peace concorde wee partes ability bounde muche maie ſithens doe yet beleeue greater moitie worlde ſtill wāteth faithe therfore hath god ordeined appointed magiſtrate beare sworde thereby curbe reſtraine wicked compellyng euen maugre willes keepe peace leaſt otherwiſe men ſhould deuoure conſume ſpoyle one office ſaie magiſtracie executeth entent worlde maie eche parte bee well quietlie gouerned heere wee ſee none euill men wee ſhould haue neede magiſtrate hee ſaieth ſainct peter puniſhment euill doer praiſe doe well thei therefore doe well liue orderlie honeſtlie ought magiſtrates handes receiue praiſe ought magiſtrate commende preferre gracifie others example maie bee prouoked drawē allured like vertue integritie thou ſhouldeſt thinke reape vnto thy ſelf merde god handes ſame ſo ſaieth paule rom xiij power bee feared good woorkes euill therefore thou wilt bee without feare power doe well ſo god well doyng ye may put ſilence ignoraunce fooliſh men theſe wordes ſainct peter ſchooleth reprehendeth thoſe vaine talkatiue perſons bragge thinke themſelues ſufficiently furniſhed euen bare name title chriſtianitie alſo herein prenēteth anſwereth aforehande obiection perchaunce thei might alledge ſaiyng faith onely bee ſufficient chriſtian workes iuſtifie purpoſe ſhould neede ſubiect vnto magiſtrate paie tribute ſaieth thus muche although wee ſhould receiue thē good commoditie yet neuertheleſſe wee bounde euen god ſake freely performe willingly yeeld obedience vnto mouthes enemy god whiche diffame ſlaunder v maie ſtopped thei maie able ſpeake againſt bee compelled confeſſe wee perſones harmeleſſe dutifull obedient ſort reade many holie men warrefared vnder heathen prince vāquiſhed ſubdued enemy thinges ſubiect ſeruiceable vnto theim leſſe wee bounde yeeld obedience vnto chriſtian magiſtrates howbeit thought ſome could bee chriſtians liued turkie ſubiection turke againe maie ariſe doubt allegation thus chriſt hath commaunded wee ſhould reſiſt euill hym ſtriketh v one cheeke wee ſhould turne thei ſaie bee lawfull v ſtrike kill men anſwere old obiection ethnickes tymes paſt alledged againſt chriſtians ſaiyng thei ſhould liue ſuche order country commonweales would ſoone bee brought ruine bee quickly ouerrunne wee vnto theſe thinges aunſwere thus true chriſtians ought reſiſt euil neither reuenge ſelues rather ſuffer violence wrong alſo cauſe thei maie chargeable burdenous troubleſome ethnikes magiſtrate inhibited sworde iudiciall tryalles although thei liue ſo orderly mā hath iuſt cauſe complaine vppon becauſe thei offer wrong man deſerue well men paciently beare whatſoeuer doen others yet becauſe falſe connterfaite chriſtians knowe chriſte theſe thinges sworde iudgement muſte bee vſe thei whiche doe hurte wrong others maie puniſhed whereby publicke tranquillitie maie bee maintained godly maie liue peace ſafetie god therefore ouer beſide worde hath inſtituted appoincted prophane ciuile power repreſſe owne accorde refraine doyng offryng harme iniurie others plainly therefore appeareth god hath appoincted inſtituted magiſtrate becauſe doe beleeue therefore chriſtians whiche adminiſter function onely maie alſo ought vſe sworde namely thereby releeue neighbour repellyng puniſhyng malefactours defendyng mainteinyng peace tranquillitie ſafetie theim bee good vertuous yet neuertheleſſe ſaiyng chriſte ſtandeth ſure reſiſtyng euill although chriſtian man beare sworde whether prince magiſtrate yet ſhould neuer vſe hymſelf neither ſhould therewith reuenge hymſelf priuate quarell owne muſt execute place office behoofe others woorke chriſtian loue sworde defende whole commonwealthe ſuffer good men vniuſtlie moleſted trodendoune chriſt gaue bequeathed doctrine theim onely beleeue haue loue ſuche dooe ſhewe forth expreſſe ſame workes ſeyng greater parte worlde beleeueth neither obſerueth precepte commaundement therefore moſte expedient ouerrule gouerne theim chriſtiās ſuche thei ethnikes panims ſtaie repreſſe ſenſuall wilfull outrage otherwiſe thei ſhould bee ſuffered runne hedlong owne pleaſures diſordred looſeneſſe lawleſſe violence man ſhould bee able liue quietneſſe ſafetie therefore bee twoo ſortes rule dominion worlde bee alſo menne twoo ſortes witte chriſtians chriſtians chriſtians gouerned worde god thoſe neede reſpecte ſelues prophane magiſtrate thei chriſtians haue neede bee vnder power rule namelie sworde becauſe thei abide obedient vnto worde god wee chriſtians obedient goſpell wee ſhould haue neede sworde ciuile power miſſeli • er malefactours vſe puniſhment▪ sithe therefore ſhould bee godlie vertuous chriſte hath committed euill vnder rule ciuill prophane power thei maie bee ſo gouerned thei ought bee gouerned beleeuers hath reſerued vnto hymſelf gouerneth onelie woorde therefore chriſtian empire againſt principalitie empire worlde neither ciuile prophane power againſt chriſt yet properlie appertaineth office chriſt yt externall outward thinge alſo office condition ſtates men bee theſe beſide mere office chriſte ſo muche infidell miſcreaunt maie aſwell beare office chriſtian ſo alſo office sworde neither maketh vnmaketh chriſtian hereof wee haue ſpoken elſwhere oftentymes large free hauing libertie cloke maliciouſneſſe seruauntes god peculiarlie ſpoken vnto v haue heard chriſtian libertie yet dooe abuſe ſame vnder colour name chriſt chriſtian libertie dooe commit dooe beſte liketh ſelues libertie ſhould breake licencious wantonneſſe carnall looſeneſſe wee ſee come paſſe day read haue happened tyme apoſtles themſelues epiſtles bothe sainct peter sainct paule wee maie manifeſtlie gather ſame dooen practized whiche adaies greater ſorte men vſually committeth wee good gifte greate fauour god dooe againe vnderſtande knowe truthe plainly ſee nothyng mere deceipte iugglyng whiche hitherto pope chergie hath taught eſtabliſhed doen conſciences thankes bee vnto god deliuered ſnares humaine tradition freed violence wherein thei entrapped v wee made free tyed vnder paine damnation doe ſuche thynges thei enioyned commaunded v libertie ought ſtande maintaine neither ſuffer ſelues drawen withall take heede wee make libertie cloake pretext wicked life therefore ſhamefullie verie vngodlie hath pope dealt behalfe preſumyng compell enforce menne lawes chriſtian people neither ought neither bee compulſion good thyng ſtraightwaies decaieth falleth doune faithe chriſtianitie conſcience bounde externall rite outward conſtitutions chriſtians muſt ledde gouerned spirite thei maie knowe firſt faithe thei alreadie poſſeſſe thynges neceſſarie appertainyng ſaluation haue neede nothyng el obtainyng thereof nexte knowe thei ought employe addicte induſtries endeuours nothing el helpe ſerue relieue neighbour thei maie euen chriſte hath holpen ſuccoured relieued theim whatſoeuer good thei thus ſhewe vnto thē thei doe freely freendly without compulſion thynges maie flowe ſpryng wel willyng chearfull harte humblie thanketh god praiſeth holie name gracious giftes ſo largely bountifully powred vpon vnto purpoſe ſerueth ſaiyng ſainct paule j timoth j thus writeth lawe giuen righteous thei ſuche doe thyng e freely willyngly without either conſtraint commaundemente thei knowe bee allowed agreable vnto good pleaſure god theſe carnall irreligious faithleſſe counterfaict chriſtians knowing bondes humaine tradition bee broken hearyng true chriſtian libertie preached come ſteppyng vaunte themſelues iollie chriſtians thei profeſſe themſelues obſerue keepe pope lawes pretendyng excuſe chriſtian libertie thei herevnto tied bound yet meant ſeaſon omitte leaue vndoen thoſe thynges whiche true chriſtian libertie requireth witte chearfull vnconſtrained helpyng neighbor thynges vttermoſte abilitie without reſpecte commaundement whiche doe true chriſtians endeuour themſelues therefore thei makyng chriſtian libertie onely cloake filthie wicked impuritie doe diſgrace pollute precious name excellente title libertie whiche agreeth onely true chriſtians doeth ſainct peter place forbid v doe effecte meanyng ſpeeches though ſhould ſaie thus although outward externall thynges ye free becauſe chriſtians ought compelled lawe obey magiſtrate law made righteous iuſte declared yet ought neuertheleſſe doe willyngly vnconſtrained neceſſitie enforced euen loue beare god benefite neighbour read matth vij chriſt hymſelf beeyng free lorde notwithſtandyng paie tribute polle money alſo obeyed pilate ſuffered hymſelf bee iudged hym whereas notwithſtandyng verie ſame place teſtified ſaied vnto thou couldeſt haue power againſte excepte giuen thee aboue whiche wordes expreſſely flattly confirmeth magiſtracie power yet ſubmitted hymſelf therevnto becauſe ſo pleaſed heauenly father forcedlie compulſion ſee theſe peeuiſhe counterfaites contemnyng aſwell thynges pleaſe god thynges whiche worlde requireth ſtill perſiſtyng wilfull way corrupte iudgementes haue right vnderſtāding knowledge chriſtiā libertie meaneth brag thei neuer ſo much religiō vaunt thei thēſelues neuer ſo gloriouſlie vnder ſhewes title goſpell wee deede freed lawes howbeeit v neceſſarily required withall wee helpe relieue weake vnſkilfull chriſtians brother whiche verie office loue wherevppon sainct paule rom xiij ſaieth thus owe nothyng man ye loue one therefore would boaſte chriſtan libertie muſte firſte performe doe partes office chriſtian witte loue helpe neighbour afterward vſe chriſtian libertie ſorte pope whatſoeuer would compell tye hym vnto lawes enioyne hym commaundement dooe maie ſaie againe sir dooe whiche giue vnto commaundement doe none cauſe would binde therevnto commaundement taking awaie chriſtian libertie impoſe neceſſitie wee muſt deale doe freely seruauntes god seruauntes men place ſainct peter teacheth v man might therby benefite ſhould require ſuche thyng handes willyngly myne owne accorde doe reſpectyng whether bee commaundement onely conſideryng waighyng brotherlie loue requireth ſame handes aſſuring ſelf thyng right acceptable pleaſaunte almightie god ſuche ſeruice dueties helpe brother ſame reaſon ſame cauſes bee compelled enforced obaie ciuile prophane magiſtrates yet willynglie myne owne accord obeye thē becauſe thei themſelues ſo exact demaunde becauſe tendeth ſerueth commoditie benefite neighbour ende ought woorkes framed thei maie iſſue proceede willyng louyng mynde thei maie bee profitable auaileable neighbour honour men commaundemente exhortation wee owe honour vnto men although wee bee free becauſe libertie ought bee readily benie alwaies doe good doe euill afore wee ſhewed many place euery chriſtian faithe poſſeſſed thoſe thynges whiche chriſtes alſo made become brother therefore euen owe maner honour vnto chriſte ſo likewiſe muſte honour neighbour thou maieſt thinke honour cōſiſteth outward geſtures bowyng doune thy bodie vncoueryng thy heade rather thy harte vnfained ſinceritie reuerence hym loue hym highly eſteeme hym euen chriſt hymſelf bee reuerenced loued highly eſteemed moreouer wee temple god ſainct paule ſaieth j cor iij becauſe holie ghoſt dwelleth v wee therefore haue ſo eaſilie caried leadde ſuperſtitious bowyng knee idolatrous hoaſt thei tearme image woodden croſſe ſhould wee muche fall doune ſhewe obeiſaunce hym liuely tē ple god ſelf ſame maner paule rom xij exhorteth v giuyng honour one ſhould goe ſo euery one ſhould ſubiect humble himſelf vnto preferre himſelf giftes giuen vnto v god vnequall ſo one ſurmounteth dignitie preeminence place callyng yet man knoweth higheſt ſight god able raiſe vp hym whiche world abiecteſt moſte ſeely eſtate aduaunce hym higheſt degree therefore euery one though worlde bee placed neuer ſo high callyng ought deiect humble himſelf yeeld honour vnto neighbour loue brotherly fellowſhippe wee declared afore apoſtles make greate difference betweene common loue brotherly loue duetie loue euen enemy belongeth cōmon loue brotherly loue whereby chriſtians loue one euen brother ſeekyng one oother commodity owne becauſe wee haue alike good giftes giuen vnto v god loue whiche sainct peter place peculiarly requireth feare god honour kyng biddeth v onely make greate accoumpt highly eſteeme kynges ruler earth withall alſo honour • although thei bee ethnickes heathen whiche thing bothe chriſt hymſelf prophetes alſo proſtrated themſelues feete kynges babylon might one ſaie mee loe thou ſeeſt place wee ought obey pope euery one ought fall downe proſtrate himſelf feete aunſwere true vſurped tooke vpon hym ciuile prophane power execute place temporall magiſtrate worldly prince doubtleſſe bee obeyed example hee ſhould thus ſaie commaunde thee weare hood ſhaue thy croune thy head vpon daie faſte thou ſhouldeſt beleeue god whitt regarded cared ſame parte thereof neceſſarie thy saluation therefore doe commaunde thee doe becauſe beyng ciuile magiſtrate prophane prince ſo mynded haue dooen hee ſhall hee doeth plaie tyraunt ſore god vicar earth onely vicegerent commaunde thee obſerue keepe embrace commaundement otherwiſe god himſelf expreſſe woordes commaunde vnder paine excommunication deadly sinne maieſt thou ſaie bee fauourable mee sir pope hold excuſed truely meane nothyng leſſe performe dooe whiche thus thou proudely preſumptuouſly commaundeſt wee bounden bee ſubiect vnto higher power obeye ordinaunces ſo long thei binde conſciences meane ſo long thei impoſe thyng vppon v concernyng outwarde worldlie thinges yea although thei plaied partes tyrauntes towardes v taketh awaie coate wee commaunded let hym haue cloake alſo thei entermeddle take vpon raigne ouer spirite leade awa • conſciences captiue wherein god alone ought ſit raigne ought rather offer heades block whit obeye ſuche poyntes ciuill magiſtrate externall empier hath power ouer erternall corporall thinges pope hath onely violently challenged vnto hym forcibly intruded vpon externall power outwarde iuriſdiction▪ alſo goeth rake catche chalenge vnto spirituall alſo whereas deede hath right neither bothe keepeth greate coyle ſetteth doune lordly commaundements rule lawes ordinaunces apparell choiſe meates college abbayes priory biſhoprikes benefice ſtaieth goeth coyneth theſe bothe synnes good woorkes therefore chriſt abide ſuche monſtruous empier meane domination externall outwarde gouernement whereby worlde ruled hee bothe liketh alloweth neither vſurpeth entermedleth thyng sinnes good workes ſpirituall dealinges dealeth altogether externall outwarde policy maintenaunce defence fortification city building making bridge appointyng aſſeſſyng tribute receite reuenues mainteinyng continuyng peace defendyng territory landes dominion ſettyng order puniſhement malefactours offendours therfore eche chriſtian maie without daunger naie willingly owne accord compulſiuely forciblie ought yeelde obedience vnto ſuche prince ſithens chalengeth authoritie ouer conſcience therefore either emperour kyng prince ſhould aſke mee faithe ought plainly confeſſe proteſt ſame vnto commaundement otherwiſe bounde confeſſe faithe openly men often occaſion offered ſhould proceede commaundyng beleeue waie waie muſte ſaie ſorte vnto hym noble prince charge reſpect externall principalitie empire looke well authoritie reacheth encermeddle kyngdome god lawfull eueroache vppon ſanie vſurpe vnto ſelf belongeth alone therefore herein maie obeye well abide ſhould chalenge right vnto ſelf within dominion yea ſhould onely paſſe rankes watchman ſetting naught though thei deale hym would ſaie ſure purſue ſuch one gūnes glaues ſtore partiall prouiſion think god ſuffer attempt pull seate ſet ſelf place sainct peter calleth ciuile magiſtrate onely ordinaunce man therfore authoritie ſtretcheth themſelues enact commaunde thing vppon statute god poinctes faithe seruants ſubiect maiſters al feare onely good courteous alſo froward thankeworthie man conſcience towarde god endure griefe ſufferyng wrongfully praiſe ye bee buffeted faultes ye take paciently ye doe well ye ſuffer wrong take paciently acceptable god sainct peter hitherto hath taught v wee ſhould ſubiect vnto ciuil magiſtrate honour wee ought giue vnto ſame diſcourſe whereof wee haue declared farre extendeth ſame magiſtrates ſtretche authoritie limited commiſſion neither ouerrule matter faithe whiche ſpoken magiſtrates generall therfore doctrine appertaineth vnto ſpeaketh ſuche magiſtracie appertaineth whole cōmonwealth certaine priuate perſones firſt familie ought bee gouerned seruauntes houſeholde ought demeane behaue themſelues towarde maiſters meanyng whiche wordes effect seruauntes men woman chriſtians aſwell others hauyng one ſame worde one faithe one baptiſme benefites beſides aſwell others therefore ſight god nothyng inferiour onely worlde externall tēporall life ſome difference reſpecte thei leſſe accoumpt eſtimation therein beeyng inferiours vnderlinges bounde waite obeye therefore ſeeyng god hath called eſtate thei ought ſo frame enure themſelues dueties thei ſhew ſubiection teſtifie ſubmiſſion vnto maiſters honour reuerence ſeruiceable vnto carefullie looke dealinges buſineſſe wherevppon prophete dauid pſalm cxxiij borowyng apt proper ſimilitude ſignifieth thereby diligently thei ought attende vnto maiſters maiſtreſſes eye seruauntes looke vnto handes maiſters eye maiden vnto handes maiſtreſſe ſo eye waite vpō lord god whiche muche ſaie seruauntes waiting maiden ought ſubmiſſion feare doe whatſoeuer maie pleaſe maiſter maiſtreſſe god requireth therefore thei ought cherefull willyng myndes doe thou thus doeſt accordyng word god faithe bee aſſured acceptable allowed god therefore theſe beſt workes al others man woorke ſo man maie perceiue hee needeth got farre dooe woorkes thy maiſter commaundeth seruaunt maiſtreſſe maide hath god commaunded doen thee think bee bare commaundement man although vttered doen man therefore thou oughteſt conſider reſpect maner maiſter thou ſerueſt whether good badd gentle curteous waiwarde churliſh thinke rather maner maiſter ſoeuer bee yet duetie truely faithfullie ſerue hym diligently applie ſelf buſineſſe god ſake requireth ſame handes remembryng alſo lorde ieſus chriſte redemption freedome became seruaunt true doctrine life whiche ought continually bee inculked beaten heades men ala blindneſſe age ſo greate nowadaies almoſte quight aboliſhed vtterlie extincte doctrine ſuche ſorte none well embrace like ſauyng onely true chriſtians haue leſſon ſame goſpell therefore thou wilt true child god frame thy mynde ſo ſerue thy maiſter chriſte hymſelf preſent commaunded thee euery particuler charge doe ſo writeth ſaincte paule ephe vj seruauntes bee obediente vnto theim maiſters accordyng fleſhe feare tremblyng ſingleneſſe harte vnto chriſte ſeruice eye men pleaſers ſeruauntes chriſt doyng god harte good ſeruyng lorde men againe expreſſe commaundemente warraunte ought doe theſe thinges ſurelie ſinguler comforte excellente benefite right precious treaſure whiche man well thinke hymſelf worthie prince maie thinke hymſelf happie al matter vſuallie doeth looke god commaundeth man willyng dooe whiche men eſtabliſhe commaunde god ſaie euery one ſeeketh followeth ſome peraduenture ſaie haue ſuche frowarde teſtie waiwarde angrie layed together one heape bee thinketh ſufficiente ſo pleaſaunte acceptable woorke god ſhall muche auaile vſe reaſons perſwade hym nothing better thou doe nothyng worſe thou forſlowe omite therefore ſaieth ſaincte peter muſt feare bee performed thynges muſte orderly duely bee executed ſeeyng cōmaundement man god hymſelf ſainct peter doubtleſſe place peculierly ſpeaketh ſuche seruauntes many tyme wit slaues ſuche ſome country yet daie bought ſolde like brute beaſtes theſe euill entreated oftentymes whipped beaten maiſters ſafely without daunger law thei liſted might kill put death therefore needefull ſuch apoſtles peter ſhould diligently admoniſhe comfort contented duetifullie ſerue frounyng waiward maiſters beare thoſe iniuries thei rigorouſlie handeled euery one chriſtian muſt needes beare croſſe pinched iniuries better fareth caſe therefore take vp kinde croſſe willyngly hartely thankyng god ſame verie true affliction pleaſeth god ſhould profite auaile thee thou arte buffered ſhreudlie beaten thy deſertes thou ſhouldeſt boaſte bragge ſufferyng croſſe therevpon ſaincte peter ſaieth ye doe well ye ſuffer wrong take paciently thanke worthie acceptable god true obedience vnto god pleaſyng worſhip behold plainly deſcribed ſet vnto thee thoſe true excellent woorkes whiche thou oughteſt doe yet fooliſhemen haue ſet naught troden vnder feete good wholeſome doctrine ſteede thereof haue deuiſed founde ſelues good woorkes inuented owne braines phantaſies whiche wee make ſuche ſpeciall accoumpt thinke neuer ſufficientlie enough extoll praiſe dignifie thē wee therefore deliuered blindneſſe taught againe whiche true right woorkes pleaſe god let v handes holden vp heauen yeelde moſte humble thankes vnto god ſo greate benefite let v hartily entirely reioyce lorde ſame herevnto ye called chriſte alſo ſuffered v leauyng v example ye ſhould followe ſteppes ſynne neither guile founde mouthe reuiled reuiled whē ſuffered threatened committed hym iudgeth righteouſlie owne ſelf bare synnes bodie tree wee beyng deliuered ſinne ſhould liue righteouſneſſe whoſe ſtripes ye healed ye ſheepe goyng aſtraie retourned vnto shepeheard biſſhoppe soules herevnto ſaieth saincte peter ye called vnto forſoothe ſuffer perſecution trouble wrong euen chriſt ſelf afore hath dooen though ſhould thus ſaie thou wilte bee true follower chriſte fitte decent agreeable thy profeſſion thou arte iniuried brabble muche repine thereat pacientlie beare take well worth conſideryng innocentlie chriſte ſuffered thynges ſakes neither exclame neither cried vengeaunce neither curſed giltleſlie brought iudge therfore thou muſt alſo looke alwaies bee iuſtlie dealt withall whollie neglecte care indifferentlie rightlie iuſtice reſpect miniſtred vnto thee thou haſte wrong offred thee ſaie rather thy wrong thanke god herevnto called ſhould ſuffer wrong ſhould complaine ſithe chriſte lorde sauiour guiltleſſe innocent euery waie complained hath saincte peter alledged certaine woordes liij chapter eſaie prophete thus ſaied committed wickedneſſe neither guile founde mouthe theſe woordes whoſe ſtripes ye healed mentioned alſo ſame chapter verſ v chriſte ſo pure ſo muche one euill woorde tongue worthie haue honoure handes deſerued bee kneeled vnto bee caried armes menne finallie power aucthoritie enough haue reuenged hymſelf ſo pleaſed hym ſuffered hymſelf rather bee reuiled mocked blaſphemed laſte put death yet opened mouthe therefore ſhouldeſt thou bee whitte vnwillyng ſuffer perſecution wrong ſith thou art nothyng synne thou ſhouldeſt rather hartilie thanke god highlie extoll gracious goodneſſe hath accoumpted thee worthie bee like chriſte repine mutter bee vnpacient thou art wronged ſeeyng lorde hymſelf neither reuiled threatened againe earneſtly praied enemy thou wilte peraduenture ſaie sall allowe thinke well deale iniuriouſly ſaie therein thei doe well aunſwere ſaie rather thus thine harte although haue deſerued hard dealing bee thus wrongfully entreated yet willyngly ſuffer theſe thynges lorde god ſake beeyng moſte innocente ſake euill entreated moſte wrongfully dealte withall commit thy cauſe god righteous iudge abundauntly recompence thy ſufferynges euen chriſt committed cauſe vnto father heauen owne ſelf ſaieth saincte peter offered vp synnes bodie tree ſuffered death cauſe owne ſake saluation wee synnes crucified nailed croſſe ala wee yet verie farre ſuche kinde ſufferyng wrong therefore thou ſincere true chriſtian thou muſte imitate chriſte poincte bee hartily ſorie hurte thee praiyng earneſtly thē vnto almightie god maie pleaſe hym forgiue theim puniſhe theim ſame ala thei doe hurte thereby ſelues soule thei doe harme thee thy bodie thou throughly conſider harte rightly waigh thou canſt chooſe preſently eaſed inward grief willyngly ſuffer thynges pacience finallie wee remember wee ſelues aſwell thei little afore ledde wicked life length tourned vnto chriſte ſainct peter knittyng vp chapter ſaieth ye ſheepe goyng hath firſte laied doune plainlie taught ſinceritie faith ſecondarily ſincere workes loue herein alſo hath hee treated twoo ſortes workes namely aſwell thoſe woorkes whiche wee bounde generalitie ſhewe ſignifieth whole entire manne euen liueth life w •• rkes fleſhe excellent order reckoned vp recoumpted ſainct paule gala v thoſe groſſe action workes fleſhe onely fornication chiefeſt greateſt vice bee idolacrie hereſies whiche bée reſiaūt bodie onely rather reaſon note therefore manne together reaſon inward motion soule bodie called fleſhe becauſe al power bothe inwardly outwardly purſueth himteth onely thoſe thynges carnall delightfull fleſhe euen ſo ſaieth saincte peter place chriſt ſuffred fleſhe whereas certaine paſſion onely fleſhe soule alſo whiche adode moſte extreme agoine whereof eſaie ſpeaketh ſame ſorte muſt alſo take followeth whiche ſuffreth fleſhe ceaſeth synne meaning whiche hath head chopped bodie onely diſmembred ceaſſeth ſynnes ſuffryng fleſhe comprehendeth ſoeuer bee aggreeueth vtterly diſcontenteth man whiche ſhalbee happe willinglie ſuffer beare miſerie calamitie vexation neceſſitie ſo euer bee greate ſorte beeyng ſounde bodie notwithſtandyng inwardly mynde greatly perplexed diſquieted harte greeuouſly tormented theſe grieues laied vpon chriſtes cauſe good commobious afflicted fleſhe ſaith ceaſſeth synne purpoſe croſſe profitable becauſe thereby synnes qualified greatly alaied manne beginneth earneſtly verie bottome harte repente wonderfull ſee ſoone quickely luſte enuie hatred ſynnes doe vaniſhe awaie ceaſſe wherefore god hath laied croſſe v hath beeyng vpon earth entire power kyngdome chriſte ſhall haue continuaunce force till laſte daie ſhall worlde begiane chriſte ſhall deliuer vp kyngdome vnto god father whereof ſpoken paule j cor xv chriſte firſte fruictes thei chriſte whiche ſhall bee commyng ſhalbee ende hath deliuered vp kyngdome god euen father c againe thynges ſhall bee ſubdued hym ſhall sonne alſo hymſelf bee ſubiecte vnto hym ſubdue thynges vnder hym whereto tendeth kyngdome god father preſence thynges alſo ſubdued vnto hym aunſwere paule ſelf ſame place expoundeth hymſelf yeldeth reaſon wordes ſaiyng god maie ſoeuer man longeth ſoeuer deſireth haue ſhall god bee vnto hym peter ſaied afore maie bee partaker diuine nature therefore god hath ſame ſhall haue ſoeuer needefull neceſſarie v ſhalbee miniſtred vnto v ſoeuer manne requireth wiſedome righteouſneſſe fortitude life ſhalbe giuen v wee beleeue hearyng eares truely poſſeſſe worde god ſhall woorde ceaſſe soules ſhall open diſplaie themſelues ſhall ſee feele thynges preſent bothe peter paule meane power chriſtes kyngdome beareth aucthoritie dooeth woorde raigne exerciſe empire whiche woorde raigneth humanitie ouer deuilles synne death helle theſe thynges ſhall till laſte daie bee plainly manifeſted although god doeth raigne euer alwaies yet ſame manifeſtly v apparaunced ſeeth v ſee hym therefore behooueth chriſt ſhould reſigne kyngdome ouer ye take heede vnto light ſhineth darke place vntill daie dawne daie ſtarre ariſe • n harte commeth peter nerer matter whiche ſaieth verie meanyng preache vnto ende conſciences maie bee ſurely ſettled ſtrengthened truthe harte maie firmely fixed vpon ſame ſuffryng ſelues bee caried ware meanes becauſe wee doubte wee haue verie pure ſincere worde god goſpell matter greate waight importaunce therefore ought moſt diligent carefull preciſe wee keepe retaine ſame ſincerelie ſoundlie without addyng thyng therevnto myng • ng falſe erroneous doctrine therwith therefore peter afterward hencefoorthe haue ſuche prophetes old teſtamente iewes prophete properlie hee bringeth glad tidynges ieſus chriſt although many prophetes old teſtament prophecied alſo matter come yet thei came ſent god peculiarly ende purpoſe preache foretell chriſte thei beleeue chriſte prophetes thei haue chief head thing whiche prophetes ought haue although al haue gift propheciyng euen faithe one ieſus chriſt wee brother kynges prieſtes ſo alſo chriſte wee prophetes wee vtter declare thoſe thinges appertaine glorie god chriſtian life wee alſo ſo farre needefull expedient v foretell thynges come ſhall bee daie generall iudgement wee ſhall riſe againe dead finally wee vnderſtande whole scripture witneſſeth paule ſaiyng maie prophecie one one j cor xiiij therefore ſaieth peter thus haue ſuche worde prophetes ſure inough ſelf onely ſee ye bee firme ſure ye dooe well ye take heede vnto though ſhould ſaie verie neceſſarie expedient ſtande ſure fareth v caſe goſpell muche like dooeth man taken encloſed darke houſe midnight neede haue candlelighte till bee daie light hee maie ſee whiche waie goe euen ſo goſpell candle midnight darcke whereas humaine reaſon wiſedome nothyng mere errour blindneſſe worlde nothyng el kyngdome darkeneſſe darkeneſſe god lighteneth v candle wit glorious goſpell whiche directeth ſteppes aright wee maie ſee whiche waie goe walke worlde till ſuche tyme woorde god neither let whit mooue thee gloriouſlie galantly ſo euer thei couche ſmothed reaſons thou feeleſt ſeeſt worde god bee abſent doubt thou heareſt mere blindnes erroneous darkenes neither lette thyng mooue thee thei b • agge ſaie thei haue holie ghoſt thei haue spirite god haue word god therefore thei doe nothyng el call light darkeneſſe darkeneſſe light ſaied eſaie v woorde god goſpell whereby wee chriſt redeemed sinne death hell harkeneth giueth eare therevnto hath linke lampe lighted kindled harte may ſee enlightened taught duty appertainyng ſoeuer lampe abſent wee fall nothyng mere darkeneſſe aucthours whereof haue light neither thei abide light therefore thei muſt needes remaine darkeneſſe continue blindneſſe light teacheth v ought doe thinges needefull neceſſarie saluation whiche poinctes farre differyng wiſedome ſkill worlde wee daiely ſtande greate neede light muſt giue heede vnto euen till laſte daie afterwardes ſhall neede worde longer candle wont quenched put broad daie light appeared ye firſt knowe propheſie scripture priuate interpretation propheſie came olde tyme man holie men god ſpake moued holy ghoſt herein peter beginneth oppugne falſe erroneous doctrine word meanyng foraſmuch ye knowe wee haue worde god cleaue faſt vnto ſuffer ſelues bee ſeduced falſe teacher although thei come ſaie thei haue holy ghoſte know ye firſt propheſie scripture priuate interpretation note ſaiyng therefore well thinke ye ſhall euer bee able owne reaſon induſtrie expounde explane scripture hereby throwne doune grounde proper priuate interpretation father ſtrait charge giuen contrarie man ſhould relye leane ſuche explanation either hierome auguſtine father interprete expounde place scripture themſelues owne deuiſed gloſes ſame diſſonant doctrine contained textes ſacred scripture vtterly refuſe thoſe interpretation peter doth forbidd man interprete expound scripture ſpirit true explanation thereof woorke holie ghoſt muſt interprete expounde ſame el muſt left without interpretation therefore aunciēt father auerre iuſtifie interpretation expoſition scripture thereby prooue place whiche expoundeth ſo bee taken vnderſtoode reuerently accept embrace ſaiynges bounden beleeue hym within compaſſe cenſure alſo wee maie ſee peter noteth nippeth ſpirites thoſe greate rabbines doctor countenaunce credite accoumpted reputed beſt graueſt clerkes therfore muſt holden firme generall rule man whoſoeuer interpretyng ye scripture owne humour bee credited although alledge bryng scripture hymſelf becauſe true senſe thereof meanes bee attained founde doltiſheneſſe wee haue verily thought pope rable chapleins mūkiſhe clergie could erre thei whiche ſhould ought haue kept v errour firſte taught doctrine vnto v wee learne wee vnexcuſable wee beleue amiſſe followe allow falſe erroneous doctrine ignoraunce ſhall excuſe v ſeeyng wee haue ſo diligently warned aforehande god hath expreſſely charged euery one ſhould bee able iudge whiche preached giue reaſon doctrine whiche hath receiued wee neglecte make ſmall accoumpt thereof wee forlorne caſe ſhal auaile v ſaie plead ignoraunce daunger leſſe hazarde loſſe ſaluation soules therefore behooueth ende euery one might plainly ſee thei whō peter meant vſeth ſame verie woorde falſe teacher falſe doctours maiſters ſaieth falſe prophetes falſe apoſtles whiche priuilie ſhall bryng damnable hereſies hereſies sectes vowed order profeſſions life therefore calleth damnable ſoeuer haltereth hym ſelf ſame damnable caſe ſtate perdition thei ſhall priuillie ſaith bring hereſies sectes thei ſhall openly ſtampe altogether diſcrepant derogatorie right honour worſhip due vnto god therefore greate difference betweene preachyng directly againſt chriſte preachyng couertly hypocriticallie vnder colour truely worſhippyng chriſte example ſhould thus preache chriſte soonne god perfect god perfect manne beleeueth hym ſhalbee ſaued preachyng true aduouchable goſpell scripture another ſhould come preache thus chriſte sonne god neither euer incarnate faithe doeth iuſtifie maner preachyng moſte falſe moſte directly contrarie vnto truthe ſuche plaine palpable godleſſe doctrine peter doeth place ſpeake neither dooe papiſtes munkiſhe mawmettes ſo groſſelie deale thei priuilie coigne counterfaicte kinde doctrine foiſte among v ſteede true ſounde religion thei ſaie thus true chriſte bothe perfecte god perfecte manne ſuffred death ſinnes whoſoeuer beleeueth cā ſaued theſe ſuche like article thei affirme bee true ſo doe thei holde thei appertaine ſerue vulgare common ſorte people lett v therefore ſaie thei inſtitute ſome perfecter waie preciſer trade life let v binde men vowe chaſtitie pouertie obedience profeſſed rule let v teache builde abbaies monaſteries celles hermitage lette v flatly perſwade thei zelouſly deuoutly doe ſame thei ſhalbe ſure aſſone breathe body goe ſtraight heauen theſe ſuche like dotage preached colorablie inſtilled mennes myndes nothing excellent bleſſed virginitie nothing meritorious counterfaite feigned obedience mū kes freers liue farre better perfecter life others theſe poinctes open defiaunce flat woordes made againſt ſinceritie chriſtian doctrine herein neither faithe baptiſme expreſſelie denied neither yet doe thei renounce denie chriſte bee sauiour worlde yet neuertheleſſe doctrine truthe couertly impugned clouded deuiſes mannes ſaluation except direction ye chriſtians ſaie thei confeſſe enough ye muſt doe ſuche ſuche good workes ye muſt build church honor sainct ye muſt erect founde monaſteries abbayes ye muſt buie certaine trentalles maſſes ſaied ſong ye muſt pyue awaie ſelues faſtyng ſuche like thus haue ſéely poore people beguiled thus haue thei perſwaded brought ſhew themſelues well likers theſe trumpery thinkyng kynges high waie heauen theſe rotten workes blinde deuotion workes beſt becauſe ſawe caried tytle church allowe followe ſame ſo proceſſe tyme grewe bee many faction sectes religion city yea almoſte men whereas ſhould rather haue taught thus ye chriſtians aſwell thei bee hundred myles diſtant ye haue one chriſt one baptiſme one faith one spirite one worde one god worke ye ſelues able doe towarde ſaluation able bring perfection right chriſtian doctrine might generally bee preached men ſhould kept fellowſhippe vnitie one common faith neither would bee difference thinges appertainyng god would alike one ſame communion vnitie thei haue broken diſioynted thei ſeduce miſleade v teachyng v wee muſt merite heauen workes drawyng v thereby faith phariſ • icall deedes peter wordes therefore bee well marked ca • ie meanyng ſhall ariſe among sophiſticall scholemen doctor teacher prieſtes munkes ſuche like beyng offall skumme worlde ſhall bryng pernicious ſectes odible order damnable hereſies ſeduce worlde lying falſe doctrine theſe theſe doubtleſſe thei apoſtle ſpeaketh thei thus perſwaded verely beleeue willfully profeſſed order meritorious thē ſhall bryng ſaluation perſwade others alſo put confidence truſt opinion would thinke thei would rather liue free abroade thei cage empound themſelues cloyſters priſons euen denying lorde hath bought thei readie ſaie thei doe denye lord queſtion demaunded thei meane ſeeke get theſe vowed profeſſiōs thei beleeue thei ſaie thei doe redéemed chriſt ſinnes waſhed awaie bloud thei quickly aunſwere forſooth faith alone ſufficient therefore muſt haue helpe good workes thus mouth confeſſe god harte flatly renounce hym conſider alſo pithie vehement word peter vſeth denye ſaieth lord hath bought thei ought bee ſubiect vnto hym vnto ſupreme souereigne lord whoſe inheritaunce thei dooe beleeue lorde redeemed worlde ſheadyng precious bloud redeemed thei cannot doe beleeus neither dooe thei acknowledge take hym lorde thei ſaye confeſſe hath bought redeemed yet thei perſwaded enough ſufficient becauſe thei muſt thei ſaie diſcharge ſatiſfie ſinnes work anſwere maie wel made thou canſt doe worke take awaie thy synnes good hath chriſte death doen vnto thee bee twoo chriſtes take awaie synnes hee good right muſt bee acknowledged onely redeemer taker awaie sinnes whiche beeyng graunted bee true moſte true thou thy ſelf canſt dooe maner worke take away thy ſinnes thou goe think whit thy work merite heauen thou canſt truly ſaie thou beleeueſt taketh awaie thy sinnes flatly denye chriſte although theſe fellowes doe acknowledge chriſte bee lorde yet doe denye bought thei beleeue ſitteth heauen lorde takyng awaie sinnes whiche proper peculier office thei nippe take quite hym attribute vnto owne woorkes meanes leaue nothyng hym bare name tytle aſcribyng power woorke vertue office vnto themſelues therefore chriſt moſte truely foretolde ſhould come many name ſaie chriſt ſhal deceiue many math xxiiij mar xiij theſe iuſticiaries meritemongers thus tying saluation woorkes ſhewe foorth ſo doyng though ſhould ſaie called chriſte chriſt whereby thei ſnatch applye vnto themſelues office whiche onely proper peculier vnto chriſt ſo thruſt chriſt ſeate place themſelues therein ſo euidently knowen man truely denye therefore worthily doeth peter tearme damnable pernicious hereſies thei leade man ſtraight reſpecte dooe deale haue exempted themſelues due obedience ciuile magiſtrates affirmed themſelues ſubiect vnto yea thei haue onely exempted themſelues due ſubiection lawfull obedience vnto magiſtrate thei alſo moſte arrogantlie haue made ciuile magiſtracie ſubiect vnto thē haue trodden vnder foote withall moſte impudently ſuffer theimſelues bee called lordes ouer kynges prince pope alſo calleth hymſelf lorde bothe heauen earth braggeth hee hath handes bothe sweardes spiritual temporal euery one ſhould fall doune hym kiſſe feete alſo ſaieth peter thei feare ſpeake euill theim bee dignitie hath hitherto plaiyng matter tricke ſmall regarde pope pleaſure curſe kynges prince depoſe theim regall crounes aucthorities pope hath thing vſual familier ſet prince together eares ſowe inextricable diſcorde warre diſſenſion betweene reſiſted withſtoode bloudie tyrannie hym thei ſhortly ſuppreſſed ſnatched vp one committed thyng repugnainte contrarie chriſtian charitie rebellious childe wicked member would enthrall ſubiect himſelf see rome kiſſe feete italian prieſte pope whoſe power thei affirme ſo farre ſurmounte excell dignitie earthly kyng ciuile magiſtrate sunne brightneſſe light exceedeth moone farre heauen higher earth beholde howegregiouſly thei blaſpheme impiouſlie thei lye thei ought ſubiect ſhewe humble obedience vnto kinges magiſtrates bleſſe thē praie chriſte ſhewed obedience pilate paied tribute vnto caeſar ſhake yoke obedience bee aucthours seedemen al obſtinacie rebellion contempt diſorder thei ought hearyng euill ſpoken againſt prince magiſtrates beyng placed ſoueraigne dignitie tremble thei ſo ſhameleſſe ſo graceleſſe ſo voide reuerent awe duetifull feare thei moſte ſaw • ily malapertlie theimſelues without feare blapheme ſpeake euill theim waighyng brute beaſtes led ſenſualitie made bee taken deſtroyed ſpeake euill thoſe thynges whiche thei know ſhall periſhe owne corruption ſhall receiue wage vnrighteouſneſſe calleth brute vnreaſonable beaſtes paine labour makyng others labour meane cauſe pretende alledge themſelues thei ſhould thus dea • e haue none ſauyng forſooth thei muſt chaunt ſing pipe god daunce churche pray god hath expreſly inordinate luſtes neuer diſſolute haunt ſinne ſatiſfied glutted wearied cauſe thei continually giuen ryot bellicheere conclude boldly impunely doe thei liſt ceaſſe ſinne pope hath cōmaunded neither themſelues winke ſhameleſſe enormious villanies others ſorte therefore haue exempted themſelues vnder power temporall sword ſo man dare withſtande againſaie lawleſſe luſtes wicked proceedinges thei liue ſo abhominablie ſo ſenſually euen gyantes tyrauntes floud beguilyng vnſtable ſoules vnder gaie glorious ſhewe thei pretende whole courſe wicked life mumbling maſſes chattering chaunting praiyng ſinging thei beguile deceiue light vnſtable ſoules want faithe herehence grewe men ſo deſired wiſſhed beecome prieſtes becauſe liked ſtate better therefore greateſt ſorte parentes thought themſelues happie could traine bryng vp child profeſſion ſo within awhile opinion commonly receiued kinde life wanted nothyng nay rather al thinges moſte plentifully abounded whereby might bothe preſent worlde liue commodiouſly delicately againe becauſe thereby thei fully perſwaded conſciences right high waie ſtraight paſſage vnto heuen would ſomewhat neerely ſifte truth founde depth matter ſhall doubtleſſe lynges ſo groſſely openly c ••• mitted none almoſte euen blunteſt 〈…〉 common people ſeeth complaineth doeth ſaie couetous haue harte exerciſed couetouſnes practiſe notablie enured acquainted therewith whiche hereby euidently appeareth haue deuiſed ſuche number ſuttle ſhiftes craftie conueighaunces whereby haue catched gotten handes wealth richeſſe almoſt whole worlde yea whatſoeuer rable monſters afterwarde beare croſſe paciently ſuffer whatſoeuer cauſe layed vpon v whereas thei teach nothing el bidd enioyne v gadde pilgrimage place place profeſſe ſelues mūkes weare frier weede become whiche loued wage vnrighteouſneſſe rebuked iniquitie dūme aſſe ſpeakyng mannes voyce forbadde fooliſhneſſe prophete ſtorie taken xxijxxiij xxiiij chapter booke nombers wherein mentioned child iſraell commyng egypt lande moabites balak king thereof ſent meſſengers syria balaam requeſt hym come curſe people iſraell whereby hee might bee able ſmite theim sword driue lande came god vnto balaam commaunded hym curſe people wherevppon balaam ſent awaie kynges meſſengers denied goe theim kyng ſente hym ſeconde tyme promiſed giue hym greate wealthe promote hym greate honour god permitted prophete goe withall commaunded hym ſpeake nothyng ſhould direct appoinct ſpeake ſaddled aſſe went waie angell lorde ſtoode againſt hym naked sworde hande whiche aſſe eſpied ſhe turned waie ſo balaam ſmote turne waie againe angell lorde wente ſtoode narrowe place waie turne either right hande lefte aſſe ſeeyng angell sworde ſtill drawen thruſte ſelf vnto wall daſſhed balaams foote againſt whervpon ſmote again· laſt ſhe laie doune vnder balaam wherefore balaam verie wrothe greate rage cudgelled aſſe ſtaffe god opened mouthe aſſe ſhe ſpake voice manne ſaied haue dooen vnto thee thou thus beateſt bounſeſt balaam anſwered ſword myne hande would ſurely kill thee aſſe ſaied maiſter thyne aſſe whiche thou haſte ridden vpon ſince firſte tyme vntill daie euer wont doe thus vnto thee lorde opened eye balaam ſawe angell god ſtandyng afore hym waie naked sworde hande wherewith beeyng greatly agaſt would haue gone backe againe angell commaunded hym goe foreward withall gaue hym charge hee ſhould ſaie nothyng whiche ſhould appoincte tell hym balaam come kyng balak kyng brought hym high place whence might deſcrie take full viewe ſight whole people iſrael place balaam commaunded ſeuen altar bee made sacrifice euery altar wente aſke counſell lorde ſhould ſpeake lorde deliuered woordes ſo excellente parable sentence ſteede curſyng bleſſe people iſraell thrée tymes one kyng beeyng exceedyngly angrie ſaied ſent thee curſe myne enemy behold thou haſte bleſſed three tymes thought haue promoted thee vnto honour loe lorde hath kept thee backe honor balaam anſwering ſaied tolde thee thy meſſengers thou ſenteſt vnto mee thou wouldeſt giue thy houſe full ſiluer gold could ſpeake none thyng thē god ſhould put mouth notwithſtandyng afterward balaam gaue counſell balak hee ſhould deale people iſraell make ſynne againſt god becauſe hymſelf neither able curſe theim neither kyng force able vanquiſhe ſubdue theim kyng erected ſett vp idoll whiche name baal peor cauſed chiefeſt madianitiſhe woman daughter prince noble drawe allure people iſraell ſacrifice god anone beganne commit idolatrie banquet feaſte yea commit whoredome wherefore lorde beyng angrie commaunded chief heades people ſhould hanged vp sunne indignation lordes wrathe might bee tourned iſraell died one daie people xxiiij thouſande perſones miſchief brought among theim balaam couetouſneſſe money matter doeth ſainct peter ſpeake meanyng greaſed popelynges romiſhe route diſciples fauourers abetter sectary verie child balaam hee gaue peſtilente counſell erecte ſet vp idoll worſhipped whereby iſraelites beeyng drawen ſynne prouoked vengeaunce wrathe god againſt greeuouſly puniſhed theſame death ſo many thouſandes euen ſo like maner biſſhoply balaamites haue erected idoll vnder name god witte owne peeuiſhe tradition lowſie inuentions doctrine merites iuſtifiyng woorkes excludyng baniſhyng fatther thus thei ſteale awaie mennes conſciences cauſe leaue true liuyng god goe whoryng vnto ſtraunge idolles whiche rebellion diſobedience hath ſo prouoked god wrathe indignation hath long puniſhed worlde ſuche greate blindneſſe obſtinacie wherein many soule hath periſhed al whiche miſeries miſchiefes wee maie thanke none theſe graunde spirituall lordynges saincte peter therefore peculiarly properly reſembleth likeneth theſe falſe teacher vnto balaam prophete becauſe like ſo dooe thei money ſake bryng moſte abhominable id • latrie deſtroie infinite number soules verie interpretation name prophete maketh ſomewhat better openyng matter bileam balaam hebrue tongue ſignifieth deuourer sweepeſtake supper vp open mouthe deuoureth gulleth vp cōmeth hand beaſtly odious name therfore giuē vnto hym becauſe allured cauſe ſo many men ſinned whereby thei brought deathes deſtruction suche maner fellowes balaamites clergie romiſhe sinagogue day wide opē throates verie deuilles dououryng ſwallowyng vp innumerable soules sirname prophete sonne boſor whiche ſignifith fleſhe moſes calleth hym beor whiche ſignifieth fooliſhe likewiſe polleſhorne doltes blinde blockiſh fooliſhe ſeekyng beare rule ouer others haue moſte neede themſelues ruled gouerned others ſuche bee menne begotten fleſhe spirite beegetteth maner perſones thus hath god scripture properly aptly tearmed ſette liuely colour namely thereby giue v vnderſtande knowe bee thought aſſe beeyng dumme beaſte daiely accuſtomed yoke burdēs ſignifieth people whiche muſt bee content bothe bee ſnaffled brideled ſadled ridden vpon goe whiche waie thei bidden aſſe violently dealt withall greeuouſly beaten ſhe went waie forced goe ſtill forwarde till ſhe came ſuche ſtraite lane ſhee could waie either ſtarte aſide narowneſſe place goe angell withſtoode ſtopped ſo ſhe driuen fall doune poore people ſo often thei feele theim ſelues hardly dealt withall caried vnſuffe • able errours faine would goe aſide wicked waie ſtraighwaies theſe ſeducyng balaamites readie rigour violence bryng erring waie againe therein compelled enforced goe till pleaſed god open mouthes putte woordes therein ſo name praiſed euen young child doe talke whereby brainſicke madneſſe ſo notoriouſly detected though thei moſte ſhameleſſe impudent yet thei chooſe bluſhe thereat place balaamites maie fitly bee anſwered thei bragge crie accordyng wonted order meete laie people thei call thē read scripture talke conferre ſame one rather giue eare hearken generall councelles doe decree ſoeuer thei agree vpon onely bee beleeued embraced maie thus anſwere god ſpeaking poore aſſe reprooued prophete whiche ſatte backe madneſſe thei therefore beeyng infatuated harte whollie poſſeſſed couetouſneſſe marueile though god ſtirre vp poore common people declare ſhewe foorthe truthe thei hitherto haue ſurcharged heauie burdeins driuen whiche waie thei lifte none otherwiſe dumme ſeelie aſſe ſeruyng onely carie burden therefore ſimilitude ſainct peter ſheweth betweene balaam blinde popiſhe guide theſe welles without water cloudes caried tempeſt solomon xxv prouerbes vſeth ſimilitude ſaiyng manne boaſteth falſe liberalitie like cloudes winde without raine ſaieth ſainct peter place thei welles without water cloudes caried tempeſt boaſte great thing thei performe nothyng thei like welles ſtopped dried vp hauyng water yet thei beare theimſelues highly vppon title boſte themſelues bee true welles scripture calleth theim welles whiche teache doeth flowe iſſue good wholeſome doctrine wherewith soules men maie refreſhed office thei ought doe thei appointed ala ſauyng onely name ſuche thyng theim likewiſe thei call theimſelues shepeheardes whereas verie deede thei rather rauenyng wolues againe thei cloudes caried hither thither winde thicke blacke cloudes deſtill droppe doune raine vpon earth thinne light fleetyng cloudes aire whiche toſſed caried hither thither commeth raine euen ſo likewiſe doe theſe pompous prelate vaunt bragge carie loftie high countenaunces churche ſeducyng worlde owne vaint guegawes tradition beyng like light windetoſſed cloudes contented ſwaie whiche waie ſoeuer sathan lifteth carie preache ſoeuer maie likyng ſo much one worde pure ſincere goſpell god goſpell word▪ becauſe none preacheth thei true preacher teacher therefore thei v eſaie place scripture tearmed cloudes becauſe thei doe deſtill lette fall harte auditorie ſweete comfortable water god truthe mercie blacke darkneſſe reſerued euer liue euen pleaſures euery thing accordyng owne harte deſires proſpereth hath good ſucceſſe glommie daie toward ſhall come vpon euerlaſtyng darkeneſſe although thei neither beleeue feele ſpeakyng ſwelling wordes vanitie beguile wantonnes luſtes fleſhe cleane eſcaped whiche wrapped errour ye aſke bee called welles without water cloudes without raine ſith thei preache much euery peter maketh anſwere thei preach deede rayne enough enough preachynges nothyng el ſwellyng proude woordes wherewith accloye fill eares poore ſeelie people thei make beleeue thei ſpeake right good catholike whereas indeede nothyng vaine fonde childiſhe thus lubberly monkes wont braue plauſible word boaſte vaunt obedience pouertie chaſtitie becauſe thei would thought common people menne holieſt whereas doings preachinges nothyng mere iugglynges deceites colluſions hauyng theim either faithe charitie ſo alſo loftie vaine bragge ſtate office biſhoppe eſtate perfection whereas thei bee mitred ſtate dooe nothyng pompouſly ieſte ſtreates awaited vppon greate retinue suiters seruauntes though great lordes fare like prince riding vpon braue horſes like gallant caualieres without regard paſtorall charge ſauyng thei hallowe churche conſecrate altar baptize belle theſe ſuche like ſwellyng vaine wordes whole pontificiall law full thwackte peſtred thei beguile wantonneſſe luſtes fleſhe cleane eſcaped whiche wrapped errour drifte theſe welles theſe teacher none entangle catche ſnares ſelie soules ſcarcely afore eſcaped namelie child lately baptized newly receiued church waſhed ſynnes deliuered adam engraffed chriſt ſaie waxyng ſomwhat bigge thei lye awaite enſnare drawe errour thei ought rather teache principle groundes faithe charitie beare croſſe chriſt ala thei inſtill nothyng tender myndes praiſes hypocriticall woorkes whereby commeth paſſe thei ſeelie younglynges caried backe againe errour although afore thei eſcape thence doe thei thus beguile men wantonneſſe luſtes fleſhe baites dooe thei vſe accompliſhyng thereof forſooth theſe holie prieſtes monkes freers nū ne reſte thoſe marked mate dooe ſaie teache theim thei ought marie liue ſingle life vnto whiche thei binde theim faſte vowes preceptes whiche dooyng thei clogge beguile menne incenſyng incityng theim luſtes fleſhe wherein thei ſuffer theim miſerably burne without allowyng vnto theim lawfull remedie whiche god hath ordeined wee ſée peter ſpeaketh none thoſe falſe teacher buſſardly guide whiche aflote raigne like prince churche god ouer poore baptized beleeuyng chriſtians promiſyng vnto libertie themſelues ſeruauntes corruption ſoeuer manne ouercome euen vnto ſame hee bondage thei extoll praiſe vaunte holie order religious sectes ſinneleſſe profeſſions whiche ſoeuer doeth enter ſhall bee ſaued moſte swiniſh impudent dominicane thomas writeth affirming ſoeuer profeſſeth hymſelf mōke ſtate perfection wherein tyme whē newlie baptized thereby ſhall aſſuredlie merite ioyes heauen haue full remiſſion sinnes owne workes theſe ſuche like blaſphemies muſt wee liſten giue eare vnto beeyng nothyng aſhamed compare owne dirtie dreames triflyng toyes vnto faithe baptiſme whiche bee god owne proper woorkes inſtitution hauyng spirite god hym hearyng theſe horrible blaſphemies ſuffer holde peace theſe ſuche like madde concluſions impious sentence monkes doe traine vp youth withall finallie whiche leaſt poinct meruailed theim aucthours theſe deteſtable errours thei haue canonized saincted whereas theim bee true sainctes deede thei haue murthered burnt aſhes haue eſcaped filthineſſe worlde knowledge lorde sauiour ieſus chriſte yet entangled againe therein ouercome latter ende worſe beginnyng sainct peter heere proueth ſheweth reaſons thei seruauntes corruption knowe chriſte throughly truely knowe wit onely sauiour redeemer owne mere goodneſſe grace hath freelie pardoned forgiuen v sinnes knowledge wee eſcape iniquitie deliuered filthineſſe worlde whiche corruption filth hauing baptiſme renounced put againe myered throwne hedlong ſame whenſoeuer departe ſtart faith truſt owne vile work faith faileth abſent spirit preſent spirite wantyng nothing fleſhe cleanneſſe bee ſort hath fallen hitherto churche rome firſt hearkened vnto embraced pure goſpell afterward declined turned aſide bypathes mās deuiſed doctrine ſo ſwarmeth al maner abhominations become common synke blaſphemous impietie latter ende thereof therefore farre worſe beginnyng becauſe become farre deſperate forlorne ethnikes euer heard worde god better haue knowen waye righteouſneſſe haue knowen turne holy commaundement giuen vnto come vnto accordyng true prouerbe dogge returned owne vomit ſowe waſhed wallowyng myer prouerbe hath peter taken booke prouerbes solomō hath theſe word dogge turneth againe owne vomite ſo foole turneth fooliſhneſſe prou xxvj ſo alſo ••• baptiſme thei haue forſaken wickedneſſe waſhed cleane filthie life haue taken themſelues co ••• conuerſation faithe charitie afterwarde fall backe infidelitie truſt owne workes •• myere deraye themſelues againe filthineſſe formed 〈◊〉 place therefore ought wiſe bee applyed workes theſe papiſtes vſe doe auriculer confeſſion ſhrift wont thus enioyne thē whoſe confeſſion thei heard take heede hencefoorth thou bee chaſt milde gentle pacient c thei ought rather thus enſtruct teache thou haue deſire become vertuous godlie humbly praie vnto god hartie earneſt praier would pleaſe hym graunt vnto thee true ſincere faith thence beginne liue godlie departe wickedneſſe impietie thou art poſſeſſed true ſincere faith good work ſtraightwaies followe iſſue ſhalt thou liue chaſt pure remedie none ridde thee daunger ſynne although whyle thou mayeſt hide reſtraine wickedneſſe impietie thyne harte yet burſt open flame length ſeconde chapter ſeconde epiſtle wherein apoſtle hath forewarned foretolde v maner teacher falſe seducer ſhould afterward come among v miſerablie miſleade v pretend excuſe haue ſufficient warnyng aforehand howbeit wee haue little regarded therefore fault greater wee haue thus ſleightly eſteemed goſpell ſwerued ſweete doctrine comprized ſame whereby wee haue lewde liues prouoked heauier wrath god againſt v wee vnwillyng heare pope lubberly drone bee inueighed againſte monſtruous marchandize chriſtian soules bee condignely taunted reproued v taketh occaſion thereby amende owne life refourme former conuerſation tryfling matter laughyng toye ſerious caſe greate importaunce ſuche whereat harte ought trē ble quake feare theſe thinges therefore moſt earneſtly diligētly bothe ſpoken heard god moſte humbly bee deſired praied vnto turne heauie wrath plague v calamitie wretchedneſſe commeth vpon v chaunce blinde fortune ſent vnto v god plague wickedneſſe impietie paule witneſſeth ij theſ ij becauſe ſaieth receiued loue truth might bee ſaued therefore ſhall god ſende ſtrong deluſion ſhould beleeue lye puniſhment reuenge god extended periſhing onely theſe falſe counterfaite ſeducing teacher thēſelues might haue ſeemed tollerable hauyng maiſtered ouerruled whole worlde pleaſures haue caried hell whole multitude people haue beene bewitched enchaunte • ſpirituall ſorceries remedie therefore v recure miſchiefe proſtrate ſelues mercie ſeate almightie god feare humilitie moſte penitently confeſſyng faultes ſuppliauntlie imploryng diuine grace aſſiſtaunce • might pleaſe vouchſafe remoue take awaie plague v earneſt hartie praier wherewith wee muſt impugne withſtande theſe falſe deceiptfull teacher sathan aduerſarie deuill bee driuen awaie weapon ¶the third chapter ſeconde epiſtle write vnto beloued wherewith ſtirre vp warne pure myndes call remembraunce wordes whiche told holie prophetes alſo commaundement v apoſtles lorde sauiour firſte vnderſtande ſhall come laſte day mocker whiche walke luſtes ſaie promes comming ſince father died thynges continue alike beginnyng creation thei willyngly knowe heauens olde earth water water woorde god wherefore worlde periſhed ouerflowed water heauens earth whiche kepte ſame woorde ſtore reſerued vnto fire againſt daie iudgemente deſtruction vngodlie men dearely beloued bee ignoraunt one thyng one daie lorde thouſande yeres thouſande yeres one daie lorde ſlacke cōcernyng promiſe ſome men count ſlackeneſſe pacient toward v would haue man periſhe would men come repentaunce daie lorde come thief night whiche heauens ſhall paſſe awaie noyſe elementes ſhall melte heate earth woorkes therein ſhalbe burnt vp seeyng therefore theſe thinges muſt bee diſſolued maner perſones ought ye bee holie conuerſation godlineſſe lookyng haſtyng vnto commyng daie god whiche heauens beeyng fire ſhal diſſolued elementes ſhall melt heate looke newe heauens newe earth accordyng promiſe wherein dwelleth righteouſneſſe wherefore beloued ſeyng ye looke ſuche thinges bee diligent ye maie bee founde hym peace without ſpot blameleſſe ſuppoſe long ſufferyng lorde ſaluation euen beloued brother paule accordyng wiſedome giuen vnto hym wrote one epiſtles ſpeaketh theſe thinges emong whiche ſome thynges harde bee vnderſtande whiche thei vnlearned vnſtable peruert thei doe alſo scripture vnto owne deſtructiō ye therefore beloued ſeeyng ye knowe theſe thynges beware leaſt ye alſo plucked awaie error wicked fall owne ſtedfaſtneſſe growe grace knowledge lord sauiour ieſus chriſt hym bee glorie bothe euermore amen ſecōd epiſtle write vnto beloued wherwith ſtirre vp warne pure mindes call remembraunce wordes tolde holy prophet alſo cō maundement v apoſtles lorde sauiour chapter wee admoniſhed bee readineſſe euery minute hower looke laſt daie firſt peter declareth vnto hath written epiſtle theim purpoſely intent laye doune vnto foundation faith laied doune ſubſtancially effectually ſufficiently afore excite ſtirre vp admoniſhe put remembraunce thei forgett thoſe thinges whiche thei afore heard receiued rather thei ſhould perſeuere ſinceritie mynde vnderſtandyng whiche requiſite fitte expediente appertinent vnto true chriſtianitie office duetie true preacher onely teache alſo continually admoniſhe exhort becauſe ſo long wee bee clad fleſhe bloud wee haue greate neede haue worde god dwell plentifully v raigne beare ſoueraigne authoritie v whereby wee maie reſiſt motion ſuggeſtions delites concupiſcences fleſhe faithfull conſtancie valiantly ſubdue reſiſt ſtriue againſt luſtes thereof firſt vnderſtande ſhall come laſt dayes mocker whiche walke luſtes ſaie promiſe commyng ſince father dyed thynges continue alike beginnyng creation bee ſome yet daie waueryng ficklemynded caried awaie certaine reaſons ſette downe booke entituled written antichriſt whiche booke declared latter daie men ſhould fall ſuche groſſe deuiliſh errour denye god mocke deryde thei heare preached chriſte domeſdaie ſaiyng true whence ſoeuer borowed ought ſo ſtraictly bee taken though whole world ſhould fall ſuche generall apoſtacie ſo vniuerſally blaſpheme god greater parte portion thereof ſhould fall awaie ſee plainly come paſſe dailie burſt goſpell ſhall publiſhed openly preached among men many wicked ſhall wraie themſelues inward harte many ſhalbe openly detected whoſe wickedneſſe impietie ſecretly lurketh diſſimuled number adaies ſmall beleeue little nothyng latter daie neither thinke euer come ſuche mocker ſkorners peter forewarneth v tellyng v ſhould ſundrie whiche would think none life therfore would paſſe day lewdely inordinately accordyng deuiſes ſenſuall luſtes deede rome italie propheſie long ago fulfilled thei come thence v bryng opinion filthie wicked life leade ſame doe teach v thoſe country chaunce inhabite little latter daie ſuche maner men muſt needes bee chriſte himſelf foretolde matth xxiiij dayes noah ſo likewiſe ſhall commyng ſoonne man day floud thei eate drinke marie giue mariage euen vntill daye noah entred arke knew nothing till floud came tooke awaie ſo ſhall alſo commyng ſonne man litle ſame chapter bee ye readie ſuche tyme ye thinke ſonne man come againe luc xxj ſnare ſhal day come vppon dwell face whole earth againe luk xvij lightening lighteneth one parte vnder heauen ſhineth vnto parte vnder heauen ſo ſhal ſonne man daie ſhall come merueilous ſodainly moſte vnlooked worlde ſhall liue moſte ſenſeleſſe ſecuritie woorde god altogether deryded contemptuouſly ſkorned therefore ſhalbee ſigne token neere approchyng latter daie menne ſhall looſely liue accordyng owne wilfull luſtes pleaſures whē thei ſhall preſumptuouſly aſke promiſe commyng worlde hath continued thus long euery thyng ſame caſe hitherto hath ſtraunge thyng ſhall happen sainct peter therefore forewarneth v bee lightly caried awaie theſe wicked ſpeeches rather knowe thei bee vndoubted ſignes token daie come verie ſhortlie willingly knowe heauens old earth water water woorde god wherefore worlde periſhed ouerflowed water thei ſuche peruerſe frowarde perſones ſaieth thei diſdaine grudge beſtowe tyme labor learnyng truth ſo muche flearyng diſdaine thei reſiſte brought ſo muche euen reade scripture yea thei ſo wilfull obſtinate thei ſeeme either thinke know ſame thyng came paſſe alſo olde worlde noah builte arke namely earth beeyng ſeparated frō water beginnyng made woorde god againe ſame earth whollie ouerflowed drouned water menne liued ſo ſecure careleſſe thei looked harme come vnto theim neither thought deſtruction hande yet ſodainly floud couered theim whiche theſe peruerſe froward perſones willyngly wilfully ignorant plaine meanyng woordes ſhould ſaie god deſtroied worlde water terrible example declared able droune vniuerſallie muche deſtroie hauyng ſo muche ſo often plaine ſundrie wordes ſo many ſeuerall place threatened promiſed theſame heauen earth beginnyng creation woorde god thei euerlaſtyng water reſted aboue cloudes firmament ſeparated water whiche sea riuers vpō earth belowe earth ouerwhelmed ſurrounded deepe worde god parted water became drie lande ſtandyng beeyng hemmed water whiche moſes large deſcribeth saint peter lightly touched ſame worde god whereby thei made created thynges therein preſerued gouerned nature ſo ſtande remaine ſuche ſituation therefore god vnſpeakable power vpholde preſerue gouerne theim thynges would quickly come wrecke ruine bee ſonedrenched couered wholly ouerflowed water mightie thee worde whiche god ſpake whē ſaied lette water vnder heauens bee gathered one place let drie lande appeare let water depart aſide giue place drie lande maie bee ſeen menne maie dwell thereon otherwiſe ſaied afore nature water would ouerflowe couer whole earth whiche ſo commeth paſſe ſtraunge miracle among woorkes god ſaieth sainct peter theſe wilfull flouter ſtiffenecked deriders ſo peruerſe incōſiderate thei maliciouſly thinke ſkorne ſhewe honor holie ghoſt reade scripture therein ſee god keepeth preſerueth gouerneth worlde within water wherby thei might well perceiue ſee thynges handes god therefore ſithe hath alreadie deſtroied world bringing therevpon general deluge ſo alſo pleaſeth doe vnto v example thereof ought ſo greatly mooue eche one v performed whiche afore threatened ſo ſhould none otherwiſe think ſurely abide woordes doe whiche hath ſpoken concernyng v heauens earth whiche kepte ſame woorde ſtoare reſerued vnto fier againſt daie iudgement deſtruction vngodlie menne old tyme god drouned whole worlde generall floude water moſte abundaunce guſhed cloudes aboue ſpouted bowelles earth belowe euery ſide ſuche ſtreames encreaſed nothyng bee ſeene water earth accordyng nature beyng drouned couered vnder water god promiſed hee would neuer thence forthe deſtroie worlde water makyng couenaunt giuyng rainbowe cloudes ſigne thereof geneſ ix therefore nexte conſume deſtroye fire ſo ſhall nothing appeare fire aforetyme nothyng ſeene water hereof alſo paule ij theſs j lorde ieſus ſhall ſhewe againſt commyng bee impudent tooto arrogant thei deryde blaſpheme hym peter alſo epiſtle writeth ſpeaketh life defiled deformed ſinnes iniquity giuen ouer entierly addicted woorke impietie call impietie life led without faith although outwarde conuerſation bee altogether flagitious damnable euill work deede fruictes impietie impietie ſelf properly called life whiche glittereth outwardly gaie ſhew hypocriticall workes whereas harte vtterly voyde faithe suche impious perſons ſaieth lord reproue becauſe preſumptuous doctrine whiche thei boldly teache thei ſtiflie defende obſtinately maintaine leanyng alwaies owne brainſicke gloſſes conſtructions ſufferyng themſelues bee conuerted turned truthe harder flint neuer deſiſt condemnyng blaſphemyng doctrine true godlineſſe ſee liuely theſe wordes enoch paint deſcribe theſe kinde perſons ſhould foyſt themſelues churche towarde latter ende worlde whiche vndoubtly ye papiſtes euery man euidently appeareth theſe murmurer complainer walkyng owne luſtes whoſe mouthes ſpeake proude thynges man finde fault dealynges reproue vnlawful diſſonaunt worde god ſhalbee ſure bryng himſelf thereby pecke trouble murmure repine gnaſhe teeth example man ſhould leaue omit peece parte biſhoppes ordinarie ſtyle wonted tytle ſtraightwaies open throates crye contempt diſobedience waie left withſtand lawleſſe luſtes ſelfwilled dealinges thei bragge haue power bothe ouer body ouer ſoules thei haue gotten handes bothe swordes ſo bee compelled lawe dooe iuſt right man ſhould preache againſt thei hand abide haue exempted thēſelues maner taxe tribute impoſition ſo man dare touche thing belongeth vnto finallie thei growen degree tyrannie man dare preſume preache worde contrarie order peeuiſh proceeding alledge scripture againſt altogether booteleſſe ſaie none maie expoūd enterprete ſame ſauing thei themſelues meanes come paſſe place thinges liue licentiouſly thei liſt theſe ſaiynges bee wreſted applied againſt v profeſſours true goſpell wee reuerently dutifully ſubmitt ſelues yeeld obedience aſwell scripture ciuile power bothe whiche thei wilbe free compellable laſt al decree cannon peſtered thwacked full proude arrogant ſwellyng wordes vtterly voyde good godlineſſe hauing men perſones admiration becauſe vantage hitteth nature diſpoſitions iumpe thei iudge thinges accordyng perſon whole pope canon ye ſhall finde commaunded biſſhoppe ſhould humble himſelf beneath poore pariſhe prieſt fruictes chriſtian life whatſoeuer al thinges rather ſounde thus let curate bee vnder prieſt prieſt vnder biſſhoppe biſſhoppe vnder archbiſhoppe archbiſhoppe vnder patriarch patriarch vnder pope finallie euery one ſhould weare habite amyſe weede cowle faſhion ſhould clippe hayre ſhaue crowne beard make apparaile many benifices many prebendes might keepe c thus thei brought thinges certaine externall ceremony tradition makyng wholly occupied themſelues mere childiſhe fooliſh friuolous trifle thei greate accoūpt eſtimation yea thei iudged leſſe deadly ſinne man ſhould refuſe adore reuerence theſe boyiſhe toyes therefore well ſaieth iude place thei haue men perſons admiratiō thei lappe vp lewd loude lye vizardes hypocriſie admire thoſe gaie ſhewes viſiblie obiect eye thei neuer ſpeake woorde neither knowe thyng ſhould knowe faith charitie croſſe yet poore vulgare people ſuffer themſelues ſtill beeſotted theſe popiſhe bugges thinke themſelues doe acceptable ſeruice god giuing good subſtaunce patrimonie feede theſe filthie swine stye lewd ſenſualitie ye beloued remember woordes whiche ſpoken apoſtles lorde ieſus chriſt thei told ſhould mocker laſte tyme whiche ſhould walke owne vngodlie luſtes place alſo giueth ſome occaſion thinke epiſtle written saincte iude apoſtle becauſe aucthour hereof reckeneth hymſelf among apoſtles ſpeaketh ſo theim though thei preached long tyme whereby maie well bee thought rather written ſome godlie man read sainct peter epiſtle culled gathered theſe woordes sentence theſe mocker bee wee haue afore declared thei alſo bee walke owne luſtes onely carnall fleſhely luſtes thoſe rather ſauour horrible impietie wherin thei liue eche reſpect accordyng owne inordinate deſires neither reuerencyng ciuile magiſtrate obeiyng worde god liue ſo looſely contemptuouſly thei neither obediently acknowledge externall yet internal gouernement al lawes aſwell diuine humaine thei flatly deſpiſe ſette naught ſo flye aire middle betweene heauen earth euen thei hoiſed vp caried aloft maiſter deuill theſe maker ſectes fleſhely hauyng spirite alludeth whiche ſainct peter epiſtle ſaied ſhould come falſe teacher whiche priuilie ſhould bryng damnable hereſies theſe thei diſobediently breake aſunder vnitie faithe beyng contented common profeſſion generall appellation chriſtians wherein eche one ſerue doe good neighbour thei deuiſe inuent certaine newe vpſtart sectes owne wherby thei feigne falſe counterfaite ſeruice almightie god furthermore thei naturall fleſhly brute beaſtes hauyng spirite vnderſtandyng hath horſe aſſe thei followe iudgement nature caried awaie concupiſcence luſte fleſhe finallie thei haue worde god direct leade frame liues conuerſations ye beloued edifie ſelues moſte holie faithe praiyng holie ghoſte keepe ſelues loue god theſe fewe woordes hath briefly comprehended whole ſumme effect true chriſtianitie faith grounde worke foundation wherevpon wee muſte builde buildyng edifiyng daiely howrely profite goe foreward knowledge god lorde ieſus chriſt whiche doen operation holie ghoſt beeyng ſort builded wee dooe worke whereby purchaſe winne ſelues merite saluation onely profite doe good neighbour herein muſt wee haue moſte diligent care wee continue perſeuere true ſincere loue without intermiſſion dooe theſe fooliſhe people whiche ſtaie themſelues vpon owne rotten workes deuiſe certaine peculiar sectes wherewith drawe awaie ſeduce men brotherly loue charitie lookyng forthe mercie lorde ieſus chriſt vnto eternall life hope taught croſſe commended life ought ſo bee framed ledde ſhould bee nothyng el ſeruent ſighyng longyng deſire life come yet ſo deſire longyng muſte bee whollie ſtaied vppon onely mercie chriſte vnto wee muſte ardently praie maie pleaſe hym euen owne mercie merite v take trāſlate v hence life come endleſſe ioyes euer abounde haue cōpaſſion ſome puttyng difference ſaue feare pullyng theim fier place ſomewhat darke obſcure bee vnderſtanded yet true meanyng thereof haue ye compaſſion ſome ſaue ſome ſo leade liues maie euen greeue hart ſee ſome ſo miſerablie blinded wilfully obſtinate reioyce ye miſerie neither take ye pleaſure delite lamentable miſcreauncie meddle ye atheiſme ſeparate ſelues theim haue dealyng companie ſome ye maie pull ſo greate daunger ſaue deliuer fearyng theim holding backe godlie ſeueritie deale courteouſly gentlie euen god hath dealt roughly ragyngly ſharpely mieldely charitablie dooe churliſhe ſterneſſe terrifie ſo ſpoile theim deale theim ye would thoſe lye fier ye ought carefull diligence wiſely pul ſaue thei bee contented pulled deliuered thei gentle meanes tender mercie bee borne withall pope hereticall rabbines vſe bee burned
